  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a5bdbb08-d1c4-4e92-a50c-be218b159372'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer41481616804318039">"For fractured souls are like magnets.<br/>Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss…"<br/><br/>Labeled a ‘Cursed’ woman of Eve from birth, Maddie has endured nothing but pain and repression at the hands of The Order’s most abusive elder, Moses.   <span id="freeText41481616804318039" style="display:none">"For fractured souls are like magnets.<br />Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss…"<br /><br />Labeled a ‘Cursed’ woman of Eve from birth, Maddie has endured nothing but pain and repression at the hands of The Order’s most abusive elder, Moses. Now living with her sister in The Hangmen’s secluded compound, finally, Maddie, is free. Free from the suffocating faith she no longer believes in. Free from endless years of physical and mental torment.<br /><br />Just… free…<br /><br />At age twenty-one, the timid and shy Maddie is content to live within the confines of her new home—safe from the outside world, safe from harm and, strangely, protected by the Hangmen’s most volatile member; the heavily pierced and tattooed, Flame. <br /><br />Flame. <br /><br />The man who ceaselessly watches over her with his midnight dark and searing eyes. The man who protects her with a breath-taking intensity. And the man who stirs something deep within her numbed heart. <br /><br /> But when circumstances conspire for Flame to need HER help, Maddie bravely risks it all for the broken man who has captivated her fragile soul. <br /><br />The Hangmen’s most infamous member, Flame, is ruled by one thing—anger. Plagued by haunting demons from his past, an all-consuming rage, and isolated by an abhorrent hatred of being touched, Flame's days are filled with suffocating darkness, pierced only by a single ray of light—Maddie. The shy, beautiful woman he cannot purge from his thoughts. The woman he has an overwhelming need to possess… <br />... the only person who has ever been able to touch him. <br /><br />Flame’s mission in life is to protect Maddie, to keep her safe. Until a trigger from his troubled past sends him spiraling into madness, trapping him in the deepest recesses of his disturbed mind. <br /><br />His Hangmen brothers fear that Flame is beyond saving. <br /><br />His only hope of salvation: Maddie and her healing light.<br /><br />Dark Contemporary Romance.<br />Contains explicit sexual situations, violence, disturbingly sensitive and taboo subjects, offensive language, and very mature topics.<br />Recommended for age 18 years and over.</span>

</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know...<br/><br/>Together, that’s how. They fight their way through <u>TOGETHER.</u>”<br/>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429723603r/14624262._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Flame</b> is not like everyone else. People have always called him a freak. Maybe they are right, because he is definitely wrong in the head. He can’t speak right. He can’t act right. He doesn’t get people and they sure as f*ck don’t get hi</span>
  <span id="freeText5895925610527104577" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 4,75-5 “<u>my sun, my light</u>” STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know...<br><br>Together, that’s how. They fight their way through <u>TOGETHER.</u>”<br>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429723603r/14624262._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Flame</b> is not like everyone else. People have always called him a freak. Maybe they are right, because he is definitely wrong in the head. He can’t speak right. He can’t act right. He doesn’t get people and they sure as f*ck don’t get him, either. His life is a whirlwind of screams and pain and agony. <i>And flames.</i> Scorching flames that ignite his blood and destroy his soul a little bit more, day by day. There’s evil in his veins… consuming him, choking him, invading his dark soul…and purging himself of it all is impossible.<br><br><i>So…why would someone as perfect as <b>Maddie</b> want someone as f*cked as him?</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “How can you be evil when you ignite such hope in me?”<br>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437407127r/15582812._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Maddie</b> has considered herself <b>Flame</b>’s since the day she wrapped her arms around his waist and thanked him for finally setting her free of her nightmare. She has been HIS since the day he started protecting her. She has been HIS since he started sitting outside her door, day and night, to make sure she was safe. She has been HIS since he started pacing before her window each night, and never left till morning. <b>Maddie</b> is HIS because she can finally BREATHE when she is with him, looking into his midnight eyes filled with pure rage.<br><br><i>Their sorrow, their pain, their suffering is the same. And <b>Maddie</b> knows they can erase the darkness that taint their souls with each others touch, with each others care, with each others LOVE.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>This man before me, the one my soul loved, was my safety. The man with whom I could only ever be this free and trusting.<br><br><u>The man who was mending my fractured soul…</u><br>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438953125r/15773861._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's near impossible to explain how I feel about this book, but I'll try. <b>Flame</b> and <b>Maddie</b>'s story was everything I've expected and more... Much more.<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438964983i/15775941._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>It's safe to say that it ruined me, gripped my poor heart, “threw it on the ground, stomped on it for a good while and used the blood as ink”, like Yelawolf says in his song “Johnny Cash”. I was left utterly speechless and breathing hard for air. It's just simply beautiful and incredibly heartbreaking that I don't believe anyone can stop the tears falling down their cheeks while reading it. The right word for the experience is, I believe, <b>“INTENSE”</b>. So damn intense...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I wanted him as my own. In this moment, seeing the man who had become the center of my world, breaking, I wanted nothing more than to save him. To gift him the peace he so richly deserved, even if it meant sacrificing my newly-awakened heart in the process.<br>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426958476r/14133653._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Let me warn you all beforehand:</i> <b>Flame</b>'s past will SHATTER YOU. I expected it to be dark, but not THIS...nothing like this. My poor boy has been through so much. Too much...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You, Flame. MY Flame. MY tortured boy. You gave me life and light.”<br>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431274206r/14817185._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even after all the nightmares he's suffered, and with all the ghosts still haunting him, <b>Flame</b> was just...<b>PERFECT.</b> I can't emphasize more how thoughtful, careful and loving he always was. He was a man that loved fiercely and fought for it, bravely. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438953125r/15773862._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then there's <b>Maddie</b>... I never thought this little damaged girl could be this strong! <b>Flame</b> was heart-melting, yes, but who stole the show in this book was our beautiful dark-haired green-eyed little girl, <b>Maddie</b>, for sure. She never let anyone stop her from loving the man she believed was her soulmate, and always protected him, in her own way.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“That beat, that new lease of life pounding within my chest? It is HIS. The awakening of my heart belongs to Flame.<br><br>(...) If it is my turn to be his SAVIOR, then I will happily step into the FIRE. ”<br>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432480670r/14969952.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their road is a bumpy one, but it ends in bliss, don't worry. You will all fall in love with them both, if you haven't still...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You are my anchor. You are the one I was meant to find on this earth. You are the one for me. Only you can understand me, Flame. NO ONE ELSE.<br>~ MADDIE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438953125r/15773860._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>So why not 5 stars, but 4.75?</u>
</b><br><br>The constant conversations that went on like:<br><br>—Flame...<br>—Maddie...<br>—Flame...<br><br>...kinda bugged me. (Ooooops!)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435277397r/15326418._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lastly... Can we all appreciate how freakin' AWESOMESAUCE Viking and AK are? They are the best buddies <b>Flame</b> could ask for, and I love them for ALWAYS being there for him, protecting him, trying to help people understand him. I can't wait to read their stories, as well!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434322078r/15203881._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>OVERALL:</u>
</b> Read it, bitchez. Seriously. Drop everything else, and f*cking read the sh*t out of it!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“What are words? Sometimes the flick of a pair of eyes or the flush of skin reveals everything you need to know. Words can wound. Silence can heal.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433584440r/15116164._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>P.S:</u>
</b> What the f*ck kinda ending was that?! MOTHERF*CKERRR!!! The wait for <b>Prophet Cain</b>'s book will be like TORTURE...<br><br>/////////////////////<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425311261r/13875014._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <blockquote>** ARC provided via HaveBookWillRead in exchange for an honest review **</blockquote>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1472063266" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13444755922846125541"><b>5 Burning for Flame Stars</b><br/><br/>First read Dec 2015<br/>Reread May 18 2017 and still fucking love this book<br/><br/><b> *Spoilers all up in this bitch*</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/fuckyes_zpsr8o9wgdx.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450537458ra/17441201.gif' alt=' photo fuckyes_zpsr8o9wgdx.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>“She would never want me. I’m a fucking retard.” I hit the side of my head with the heel of my palm as my eyes blurred again. “I don’t think right in here. I’m fucked up—I don’t get people, they don’t get me. And I ain’t ever gonna be able to read people. Why would someone as perfect as her want someone as fucked up as me? Someone who isn’t right in the head?”-Flame</b><br/><br/>T</span>
  <span id="freeText13444755922846125541" style="display:none"><b>5 Burning for Flame Stars</b><br><br>First read Dec 2015<br>Reread May 18 2017 and still fucking love this book<br><br><b> *Spoilers all up in this bitch*</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/fuckyes_zpsr8o9wgdx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450537458ra/17441201.gif" alt=" photo fuckyes_zpsr8o9wgdx.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“She would never want me. I’m a fucking retard.” I hit the side of my head with the heel of my palm as my eyes blurred again. “I don’t think right in here. I’m fucked up—I don’t get people, they don’t get me. And I ain’t ever gonna be able to read people. Why would someone as perfect as her want someone as fucked up as me? Someone who isn’t right in the head?”-Flame</b><br><br>Tillie Cole slayed me. Damn This book was everything I wanted and more. Souls Unfractured is my favorite book in the Hades Hangmen series. I fell madly in love with Flame in the first book. He was so broken I just wanted to fix him and make it all better. So I couldn't wait to get to his and Maddie's book. And it was better then I expected. There was some seriously dark, twisted, and taboo parts in this book, but Flame and Maddie's relationship was touching, powerful, and beautiful. This book obliterated me, broke my heart then pieced me back together. Although I am pretty sure I need some therapy after reading this! But damn it was worth it!<br><br><b>“We have been in greater danger than this in our lives, Lilah. And Flame saved me. Twice. If it is my turn to be his savior, then I will happily step into the fire.”-Maddie</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/BeFunky%20Collage_zpssbmt6srl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450537458i/17441202._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo BeFunky Collage_zpssbmt6srl.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Flame… I know you are lost right now. But I want to save you. I want to save you as you have so often saved me.” I swallowed the lump clogging my throat and continued. “I know you want eternal peace, but… but… I cannot… I cannot take your life.” Tears streamed from my eyes, but I lowered my mouth to a few inches from his ear. “I know the flames torture you greatly. And I know you live with pain. I know you no longer want to live. I…” I sniffed back my emotions as Flame became eerily still. “I have been there too. I have felt the urge to fade, to never wake again. But then something happened to me. Someone happened to me… You.” -Maddie</b><br><br>Maddie having escape only a few months ago from The Order, a religious cult that branded her a cursed devil's whore since birth because of her beauty, lives in fear. Only one thing makes Maddie feel safe, feel anything and that is Flame. Flame, the man that killed her tormentor, Brother Moses, a man that raped and hurt her daily since she was six. Everyday Maddie sits in the window watching her hero Flame pace back and forth keeping guard over her, cutting himself. She watches and wishes to help him be free of his demons as he freed her of hers. She sits in her window and draws the life she wishes she could have with Flame, a life free of fear, a life with touch and love. Since neither her or Flame can stand to be touched she knows she can never have her dream of having a love with Flame like Lilah and Ky or Mae and Styx have, so she must be content with watching him and her art. But when some unknown thing triggers a mental break in Flame, and no one can reach him, Maddie knows she must go to him and try before it's to late!<br><br><b>“Because that is my Flame in there. And he needs me. No one else. Me.” “Your Flame?” she whispered, and her head tilted to the side. I felt a blush coat my cheeks and I shrugged. “That is how I regard Flame. As mine. From the moment I was able to touch him, and he touched me, I was claimed. I have been his this whole time.”-Maddie and Mae</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/BeFunky%20Collage2_zpsp1s4d7e1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450537458i/17441203._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BeFunky Collage2_zpsp1s4d7e1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I held you, and you held me.” Her hands moved and gestured down her body. “And your touch did not harm me. The flames you believe run in your veins, did not engulf me. Instead, you gave me life. You gave me back my light.” Another tear fell down her cheek, and she whispered, “You, Flame. My Flame. My tortured boy. You gave me life and light.”-Maddie</b><br><br>Flame is one of the most broken, raw, beautiful, and memorable characters I have ever read. He is now one of my top 5 favorite heroes of all times with Bone, Vlad, Talen Kayrs, and Ian Mackenzie. I could never do justice telling how damn amazing I find him, but I am going to try. Flame grew up in a religious cult too, one that doesn't believe in doctors, one where they dance with snakes, drink snake poison, and if a snake bites you it means you have evil in you. Having always been different, Flame didn't fit in. He didn't know how to talk to people, didn't understand facial expressions, social cues, or emotions. People always cried, laughed or got angry with him. The book never says, but I am sure he is high functioning autistic. His father would get mad, beat him, calling him a evil retard, not knowing what he did wrong he just stop talking which only made is father angrier. Telling Flame that he has the flames of hell running through his veins and that he is evil. His father takes him to their pastor who tortures him and let snakes bite and hurt him. When that doesn't work, his father takes him home and locks him in the cellar, beating and bleeding him to get the flames out. His mother not being able to take her husband's abuse of her or her sons kills herself leaving Flame alone with his evil father and baby brother. This of course causes his father to hate and hurt him more. Flame blames himself for his mother's death. His father told him she killed herself, because she hated having a evil retard for a son, then he starts daily raping Flame while cutting his back with a blade . Flame is a broken man, A man so damaged he thinks his touch kills and hurts. He always feels flames under his skin, he is always cutting himself trying to get them out. Reliving daily the abuse of his father in his head til it drives him crazy. Flame wants Maddie, but he doesn't want to hurt her with his touch. Maddie is his and he will do everything in his power to protect her even if he can never really be with her.<br><br><b>“I won’t fucking hurt Maddie. I’d die first. She stays with me always. In my cabin, by my side. And no fucker will be taking her from me.”-Flame</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_nh9dbzYaGf1u2i8ono1_250_zpsyvxjz3a2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450537458ra/17441204.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_nh9dbzYaGf1u2i8ono1_250_zpsyvxjz3a2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“And I want to replace their touch with yours. I want to wake up with your arm around my waist, keeping me safe.”-Maddie</b><br><br>Maddie and Flame together are one of the most beautiful couples ever. The way they give so much to each other, fight for each other, protect each other. The way their love overcomes their brokenness. Learning what true and pure love was together. Learning to touch each other, trust each other. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They were both virgins never having touched or kissed anyone only having been raped. They are each others first true everything <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It was heart warming, and breathtakingly beautiful. Their love was worth all the dark, gut wrenching things I had to read about their past. They both have been through fire and came out together stronger then ever.<br><br><b>. “That you are my anchor. You are the one I was meant to find on this Earth.” Her finger stopped and she looked into my eyes. “That you are the one for me. Only you can understand me, Flame. No one else. You have spent your entire life lost, not understanding what people want, but with me, you always know how to make me happy. How to make me feel safe.”-Maddie</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/love%20together%20forever%20iphone%206%20plus%20wallpapers%20-%20couple%20fire%20iphone%206%20plus%20wallpapers-f40384_zps50mnrsq9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450537458i/17441205._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo love together forever iphone 6 plus wallpapers - couple fire iphone 6 plus wallpapers-f40384_zps50mnrsq9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I have to have her with me, all the time. All the fucking time.” I pounded my fist over my chest. “Can’t fucking breathe without her nearby. Need her to sleep with me. Need her to keep the flames away.” I ran my nails over the scars on my arm. “She ain’t ever leaving me again. For life, brothers. She’s mine for fucking life.”-Flame</b><br><br>I still feel there is no redemption for Cain. I don't really care if he claims ignorance in the raping of children or the punishment of Lilah. He was told about it more than once, hell he seen enough with his own eyes to know it was true. He just didn't want to rock the boat and ruin his chance at getting Mae for himself. Turning a blind eye doesn't make him less guilty. Not to mention he also knows that women have no choice in having sex with men in what is called the Lord's sharing. No choice is rape! So he was okay openly with the rape of the women in The Order. So in my eyes he is not only a disgusting, repulsive bastard , but he is a coward and pussy too. Is it wrong that when his brother Judah betrayed him that I was laughing at him, enjoying the little bit of comeuppance Cain got while wishing it would have been worse? Will I read his book? You bet I will. Why because I have OCD and I won't be able to skip around, and I want to read the series I fell in love with all the way through. Plus I now hate his brother Judah too and want to see them both suffer. <br><br><b> “I did not know they did that. I did not declare that to be her punishment.” Mae’s eyes fell lovingly on Delilah and she asserted, “But you did nothing to stop it. You left your brother to conduct his own form of punishment, at least that was what Lilah told me. And he did. You gave him free rein to torture an innocent woman.” -Cain and Mae</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/17347349_zpsmlrsh87n.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450537458ra/17441206.gif" alt=" photo 17347349_zpsmlrsh87n.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I lost everyone. He fucking took everyone from me. My mama, Isaiah. He fucking took me from me. Made me into a psycho freak. All my life I’ve had nothing. He fucking took it all. I… I never stood a chance.” My stomach sank as I felt every ounce of his pain. Flame suddenly stilled and stared at me, as though I were a living miracle. “Then I got you. I have you, and I can’t lose you, Maddie. I can’t ever fucking lose you or I will fucking go insane.”-Flame</b><br><br>I am so glad I found this amazing series and I can't wait til the next book comes out, because I am already craving more! <br><br><b>“I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that’s how. They fight their way through… together.”-Maddie</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13444755922846125541" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1086916132" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1086916132" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1086916132?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1086916132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4573671387084968223"><b>5 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/8543d3af-327e-46a3-bb93-01e2fbdca98f_zpsl9kcuw8x.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439200696i/15807258.jpg' alt=' photo 8543d3af-327e-46a3-bb93-01e2fbdca98f_zpsl9kcuw8x.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Tillie Cole is one of those authors I can always count on to make me feel when I read. She does an amazing job of writing tortured characters with emotional and beautiful stories. <i>Souls Unfractured</i> may be her most emotional book yet. Although I knew it would be. After hearing about the things Maddie (Mae’s sister) went through in the previous books, I knew her story would get to me. Pair that with Flame, who’s past may have been even more horrid and you’ll have a book that will keep </span>
  <span id="freeText4573671387084968223" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/8543d3af-327e-46a3-bb93-01e2fbdca98f_zpsl9kcuw8x.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439200696i/15807258.jpg" alt=" photo 8543d3af-327e-46a3-bb93-01e2fbdca98f_zpsl9kcuw8x.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tillie Cole is one of those authors I can always count on to make me feel when I read. She does an amazing job of writing tortured characters with emotional and beautiful stories. <i>Souls Unfractured</i> may be her most emotional book yet. Although I knew it would be. After hearing about the things Maddie (Mae’s sister) went through in the previous books, I knew her story would get to me. Pair that with Flame, who’s past may have been even more horrid and you’ll have a book that will keep your heart hurting, but in true Tillie fashion, it will be healed by the end of the book. <br><br>Flame is one of those characters who I had to know about after reading the first two Hades Hangman books. He’s different than the rest of the Hangmen. He’s a little more violent, a little more quiet and there is something different about him… he can’t be touched by anyone. Not women, not his brothers that he trusts. He can’t cope with that. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/85bc66d8-ddc4-4692-af4d-8123d97afe8b_zpstiqjs45x.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439198456i/15807060.jpg" alt=" photo 85bc66d8-ddc4-4692-af4d-8123d97afe8b_zpstiqjs45x.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>He and Maddie have that in common. Maddie grew up in the same religious cult as Mae and Lilah. The man who had her was extra violent and terrible and has scarred Maddie. Men make her nervous, even good men. All men. All men, except for Flame. He saved her and she isn’t afraid of him. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I did not fear you. I fear a man’s touch. I find it abhorrent. But not yours. I wanted to embrace you that day. I needed to. Even if we cannot ever embrace again.”</blockquote>
</i> She dreams about being with Flame, about touching him. Even the most simple thing, like holding hands would mean the world to her. And this is not one sided. Flame wants more than anything to be able to touch Maddie. To be there for her when he needs her, to be able to hold her, but he’s not sure it’s possible. He cares too much for her to ever hurt her the way he feels he will if she gets too close. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/baff447a-6dde-4e7b-9003-b1f2fcca51b5_zps2paip5vp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439198456i/15807061.jpg" alt=" photo baff447a-6dde-4e7b-9003-b1f2fcca51b5_zps2paip5vp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maddie and Flame are characters who grow together, who go through hell together, and who heal together. Watching their story unfold was such a beautiful and emotional experience. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I know I’m different. I know I don’t see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if it’s the only one I’ll ever understand.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> I loved these two broken characters so much. I rooted for them. I was proud of them when they overcame things that were hard for them. Their story was not easy to read. Especially Flame’s. I could tell pretty much straight away why he was the way he was and knowing how he was treated growing up made me sick to my stomach. It’s not an easy read. But by the end, it’s so worth it. Maddie and Flame’s love story is worth all the heartache. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “I understand you Flame. And I am beginning to understand myself. What you and I are to each other.”<br> “And what is that?” I asked gruffly.<br> Maddie bowed her head. “Everything.”<br> My heart missed a beat, then she lifted her head and said, “Love.”<br> Maddie’s hand dropped over her racing heart and she whispered, “You, to me, are the only one I could ever love.”</blockquote>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/c6bb9906-cf78-450c-a562-0f873a2a0585_zpsvdmzygn2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439198456i/15807062.jpg" alt=" photo c6bb9906-cf78-450c-a562-0f873a2a0585_zpsvdmzygn2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maddie and Flame are characters that touched my heart and ones I won’t ever forget. Not only did we get to know so much more about them, but we also got more Ky and Lilah, Styx and Mae and getting to know AK and Viking makes me want their books next! I love the friendship and brotherhood they had with Flame. And call me crazy, but I’m dying to know whats going to happen with Cain as the series continues… <br><br><i>Souls Unfractured</i> is another fantastic addition to the Hades Hangman series. These books are so much more than just biker books. They are stories of overcoming adversity, healing old wounds, moving on from the past and letting love conquer all. Tillie Cole is a favorite author of mine and books like thing just solidify that. Full of a beautiful intensity, her words move you, make you feel, break you apart, then heal that broken heart. This was a real win for me and I’m looking forward to reading the next book in this series! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I used to wonder how two people- one broken girl, and one broken boy- could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that’s how. They fight their way through… together.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/dd7f1c3e-0032-4777-a4aa-643c06e949b4_zpsxs0puwpi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439199033i/15807082.jpg" alt=" photo dd7f1c3e-0032-4777-a4aa-643c06e949b4_zpsxs0puwpi.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4573671387084968223" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1044265133" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer95494980707865349"><b>4 - 4.25 "Not Gonna Lie, That Sketch Was Wack, But I'll Take It" Stars</b><br/><br/>So...I'm gonna be frank with ya'll and admit that I don't really know what I want to say about this book. <br/><br/>I - like a <i>lot</i> of people - have been looking forward to Flame's book since I read book one. And as a result, my anticipation for this thing - NO MATTER HOW HARD I TRIED TO TEMPER IT - was through the effin' roof. <br/><br/>Thus...enter my love/hate friend "Too High Expectations."<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439316860i/15821617._SX540_.jpg' width='368' height='209.5' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Now, typically when this asshat shows up, the book end</span>
  <span id="freeText95494980707865349" style="display:none"><b>4 - 4.25 "Not Gonna Lie, That Sketch Was Wack, But I'll Take It" Stars</b><br><br>So...I'm gonna be frank with ya'll and admit that I don't really know what I want to say about this book. <br><br>I - like a <i>lot</i> of people - have been looking forward to Flame's book since I read book one. And as a result, my anticipation for this thing - NO MATTER HOW HARD I TRIED TO TEMPER IT - was through the effin' roof. <br><br>Thus...enter my love/hate friend "Too High Expectations."<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439316860i/15821617._SX540_.jpg" width="368" height="209.5" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, typically when this asshat shows up, the book ends up blowing huge chunks. <br><br>But, thankfully, Tillie Cole is a badass and this thing still managed to rise to the occasion I had party-planned in my mind. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439317734ra/15821745.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So a little about the book...<br><br>We get some major glimpses into Flame's childhood, which were super awful and sad - but I was expecting that, because: <br><br>a) How else would he have ended up so fucked up?, and <br>b) A little birdie told me that would be the case. <br><br>Needless to say, if you have certain...triggers...you might want to skip this one or simply skim parts of it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439317549i/15821734._SX540_.jpg" width="550" height="421" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Personally, however?<br><br>Yes, there was some AWFUL shit in this book - in both Flame's past and Maddie's past. <br><br>But like I've said before:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439317549i/15821735._SX540_.jpg" width="600" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, while yes, at first I was a little bit like this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439317549ra/15821736.gif" width="500" height="263" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>After about the third or fourth flashback...?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439317549ra/15821737.gif" width="480" height="330" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So sorry, so heartless...<br><br>Luckily Flame was a super vengeful badass.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439318231i/15821803.jpg" width="512" height="512" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Which was effi'n <i>fun</i>. <br><br>But I digress. <br><br>Maddie and Flame were super cute in this book and it was really beautiful to watch them come together the way they did. <br><br>I <i>will</i> admit, however, that there was something just missing for me in this book - between Maddie and Flame - that I can't really explain - thus my not giving it 5 stars.<br><br>But that's probably just me. <br><br>Otherwise?<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434930223ra/15279638.gif" width="245" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And, of course, now I can't wait for the next one. <br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br><b>The wait for this <i>might</i> actually kill me. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437588144ra/15600291.gif" width="500" height="265" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br><b>So random thoughts I was having this morning...because I think about random crap <i>most</i> of the time...not that anyone gives a hoot, but still.<br><br>***Unnecessary Thought Sharing Alert*** <br><br>I've always pictured Mae as Mila Kunis:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434730135i/15256892._SY540_.jpg" width="340" height="444" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And since I always thought Sarah Hyland could pass as her little sister, she's my Maddie...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434730135i/15256893.jpg" width="400" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Boom.</b><br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br><b>August?????!!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429796132ra/14631250.gif" width="500" height="374" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>And the waiting begins. Again.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409755338ra/11017293.gif" width="389" height="235" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Make it come faster, Samantha.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418741728ra/12886334.gif" width="400" height="297" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

WHAT NONSENSE IS THIS!<br>ONE CANNOT WAIT SO LONG FOR A BOOK THAT IS DEARLY ANTICIPATED!!</b><br><br><b>Mysterious. Tattooed. Scarred. Angry. Cuts for pleasure. Hades Hangmen biker. Flame</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393771048i/8761153._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Beautiful. Broken. Young. Ex-cult prisoner. Maddie</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404605087i/10263461.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>'<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22020052.It_Ain_t_Me__Babe__Hades_Hangmen___1_" title="It Ain't Me, Babe (Hades Hangmen, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">It Ain't Me, Babe</a> by Tillie Cole Extract:</b><br><br><blockquote>"Who killed him?" she asked tightly, he green eyes running down the line.<br>On the end of the line, Flame begin to twitch his head, his heads balling into fists. Fuck. It had to be Flame, didn't it? This weren't gonna end well if she started shooting off her mouth.<br>Maddie fixed her gaze on Flame. "Was it you?" she asked frankly.<br>Flame nodded once and his mouth tightened.<br>"Yeah, I killed the fucker." His tattooed orange flames danced on his tense neck as his crazy black eyes fixed on Maddie. A fuckin' murderous glare.<br>Maddie stood right in front of him-<i>brass balls</i>, I thought as Flame's chest jerked erratically. Then, suddenly, <b>she released a choked sob and threw her arms around Flame's waist.</b><br>Flame froze and his black eyes widened to the size of plates. <b>His hands shot up in the air clenching into fists.</b> <i>Fuck!</i> <b>The brother couldn't be touched.</b> He was about to go nuclear.<br>"Thank you," Maddie whispered and pressed her cheek flat to his cut. "Thank you so very much..."<br><b>Flame's eyebrow pulled down in confusion</b> and his <b>black eyes glared down at her wrapped 'round his waist.</b> Then we all froze as <b>his hands lowered and flattened awkwardly on her back.</b> His nostrils flared as Maddie released another sob and cried.<br>"You freed me. You freed me from him."<br>Flames <b>eyes squeezed shut and his teeth clenched</b>. But he <b>didn't push her off, didn't scream, jerk, or hit out.</b> The <b>fucked-up brother just let it happen.</b><br>Ky turned to me, shock clear on his expression I shrugged. I could never get a read on the brother. Never knew what the fuck he was thinking.<br>Maddie pulled bak with a small smile and Flame's eyes bored into hers. She began walking back to Mae, but not before glancing over her should. "What is your name?" she asked Flame nervously.<br>Flame's lips parted and released a hiss of a breathe before muttering. "flame."<br>Maddie smiled a wide, stunning smile. "You have my <b>eternal gratitude</b>, Flame. <b>I am forever in your debt.</b>"<br>Flame <b>stared and stared at Maddie</b>, a fuckin' <b>hungry expression on his face.</b>"</blockquote><br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22107044.Heart_Recaptured__Hades_Hangmen___2_" title="Heart Recaptured (Hades Hangmen, #2) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Heart Recaptured</a> by Tillie Cole Extract 1:</b><br><blockquote>"Flame swung around and fisted AK's cut. The brother didn't even flinch. AK and Vike had known Flame for years. They were the only fuckers that could understand him. "They could have killed her. For that, they will die! They could have taken her from me. The could have take <i>her from me</i>! And <i>she was screaming</i>, but I couldn't touch her!" He let go of AK, sliced at his arm, and hissed out in relief as blood dropped to the dirt. "I need to kill."</blockquote><br><b>Extract 2:</b><br><blockquote>"Flame's whole body tense, a fuckin' scary shit noise ripped from his throat, and he boomed out, "HE AIN'T <i>HER</i> FUCKIN' BROTHER MOSES! SHE'S FUCKIN' MINE!!!"</blockquote><br><b>Extract 3:</b><br><blockquote>"Flame's head was twitching from side to side and his black eye roved the yard like an animal seeking prey. A bottle of beer was thrust into his hand by Viking, but Flame threw it to the ground and continued his search.<br>Seeing us sitting on the porch, Flame stormed over, his ams and chest muscles bulging under his full body of tattoos... "Where is she?" Flame snapped at Styx before I had a chance to apologise for what I had done to him.<br>Flame next looked to Ky. This time his voice was LIKE broken glass, "Where. Is. She?"...<br>Flame radiated rage and, face turning red, he screamed, "<i>WHERE THE FUCK IS SHE!</i>"</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2015/02/15/a-tb-exclusive-hades-hangmen-valentines-novella-by-tillie-cole/" rel="nofollow noopener"> A TB EXCLUSIVE!!! HADES HANGMEN VALENTINE’S NOVELLA by TILLIE COLE!!!!</a>
</b><br>OMG GUYS READ FLAME AND MADDIE'S PART. IT'S PURE LOVE!<br><br><b>Extract:</b><br><blockquote>Just as I turned onto the porch, I saw a Harley parked up out back… a black and chrome Fat Boy customized with fucked up paintings of Hades and red and orange flames. That bike only belonged to one man… one brother I couldn’t get the fuck away from my cabin.<br><br>Flame.<br><br>The psycho brother Flame.<br><br>Walking to my door, Flame was pacing the back porch, his crazy fucking eyes wild. Hearing my footsteps sound on the wood, Flame snapped his eyes to mine, his knife pulled out ready to cut a fucker up.<br><br>When he saw it was me, the muscles in his neck twitched and he stormed my way. “When’s she back?” he said through clenched teeth.<br><br>“<i>Thirty, forty minutes</i>,” I signed back. Flame watched my hands move and his black eyes settled down, but his hands still shook like fuck.<br><br>I pushed my key into the lock and looked to him again. He was staring at his hands, a confused look on his face.<br><br>I whistled and the brother met my eyes.<br><br>“<i>You good?</i>” I signed.<br><br>Flame scraped his fingernails down his cheek, huge welts appearing on the skin that his beard didn’t cover. “Been on the road too long. Too long, Prez. Haven’t slept. Haven’t eaten… just need to see her. Can’t switch my brain off. Just keep seeing her face in my head.”<br><br>Flame’s eyes bore into mine and I nodded my head. Fuck knows what was going through his mind, but the fucked up possessive way he was ‘bout Maddie had gotten worse.<br><br>I knew I shouldn’t have taken him on that run. He was more unstable than ever. Maddie was completely fucking with his head.</blockquote><br><br><br><b>A story that is going to <u>probably</u> leave me breathless~<br>Two broken souls. One love. Flame and Maddie.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404605839i/10263497.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There's <b>excited</b> and then there's <b>me</b>:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384831449ra/6986551.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380743475ra/3118207.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1134471375?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1134471375" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4556763904030708256"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br/>{BR With My Beautiful Bestie}<br/><br/><br/><b>"I used to wonder how two people - one broken girl, and one broken boy - could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that's how. They fight their way through...</b> <i>
  <b>together."</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/a0fd1d047a2f15021655679afe2d49c5_zps3uyt7pxi.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439675421i/15870960._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo a0fd1d047a2f15021655679afe2d49c5_zps3uyt7pxi.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I LOVE the Hades Hangmen series!! I mean <b>FREAKING LOVE</b> it!!! Since book one I have been intrigued by the dynamics between Flame and Maddie! What I love about this series is that even though each book is about a different couple, all of</span>
  <span id="freeText4556763904030708256" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br>{BR With My Beautiful Bestie}<br><br><br><b>"I used to wonder how two people - one broken girl, and one broken boy - could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that's how. They fight their way through...</b> <i>
  <b>together."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/a0fd1d047a2f15021655679afe2d49c5_zps3uyt7pxi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439675421i/15870960._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo a0fd1d047a2f15021655679afe2d49c5_zps3uyt7pxi.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>I LOVE the Hades Hangmen series!! I mean <b>FREAKING LOVE</b> it!!! Since book one I have been intrigued by the dynamics between Flame and Maddie! What I love about this series is that even though each book is about a different couple, all of these characters are very much a part of the story throughout the series. So when we get to their book, we already have a vested interest in the characters. Tillie kept our interests piqued throughout the first two books where Flame and Maddie were concerned. I just knew this was going to be a very heartbreaking journey and I was ready for the challenge.<br><br><br><br><br>Flame and Maddie both have had the most horrific childhoods. We knew what Maddie's past had entailed but could only guess as to what made Flame the way he was. So full of anger. Unable to be touched by another human being. Not having the ability to hold a normal conversation with anyone, and yet he is drawn to Maddie. Ever since the day the Hades Hangmen rescued her from the cult, Flame has made it his sole responsibility to keep watch over and protect Maddie.<br><br><br><br>Something traumatic happens that triggers Flame to have an intense flashback and ultimately he loses what little sanity he had left. Maddie is the only one who is able to reach Flame. She proved to be quite a strong heroine. This <i>
  <b>little one</b>
</i>, has to be the bravest woman in the entire series. She saw past all the crazy and found the beauty that was within Flame. He may have rescued her from the cult and the ghosts from her past, but she also saved him from the chains that tied him to his painful childhood.<br><br><br><br>I found myself crying so much while reading this one. Together, Flame and Maddie have endured things when they were young children that were so horrific I actually wished that I could jump into the story and go a little Hannibal Lecter on some asses!!! Ms Cole definitely went a little easier on us in this installment than she did in book two. Thank God because I don't think my heart could have handled that level of darkness again, and I would have considered it a bit of overkill to put these characters through additional turmoil.<br><br><br><br><br>The romance was pretty beautiful and had an air of innocence. There definitely was some steam but not like in the previous installments and honestly I wouldn't have had it any other way. Flame and Maddie were really experiencing sex in a healthy and loving way for the first time. It was a miracle that they could experience beauty in something that used to be the cause of pain and darkness.<br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/71d8e2fa08cfe3a047dc59f9e06251f3_zps87ymltjm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439675421i/15870961._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 71d8e2fa08cfe3a047dc59f9e06251f3_zps87ymltjm.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>This is definitely my favorite in the Hades Hangmen series so far! I am quite curious to see what Tillie Cole has in store for us in Cain/Rider's book. I read someone's predictions on Facebook about who his love interest will be and BOY WOULD I LOVE THAT!!!! I never even thought it a possibility but I truly hope that Ms Cole has that same idea running through her talented mind!!<br><br><br><br><br>I can't say enough about this series. I would definitely recommend it, but warn you that you need a buddy reader to help you get through some of the rough parts. This is one hell of an AMAZING story!! Don't pass this one up!!!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/13408900_zpszrs82pf0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429805874ra/14632661.gif" alt=" photo 13408900_zpszrs82pf0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/giphy_zpsaxtv7ut1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439614525ra/15861358.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpsaxtv7ut1.gif" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/awesome_zpsnsc9divg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439614525ra/15861359.gif" alt=" photo awesome_zpsnsc9divg.gif" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/9148542_zps4c55cb53.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398730124ra/9456935.gif" alt=" photo 9148542_zps4c55cb53.gif" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14740746455846841401"><br/><b>4.5 Stars...</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439409452i/15832976._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I may need therapy after this damn book. For the faint of heart...it certainly is not. More than once I had to stop reading, overwhelmed, I had to remind myself certain characters weren't real, so I couldn't hunt them down and destroy them - I couldn't make them suffer, over and over... Gah. Even now, thinking about some of the stuff I read, my blood pressure is probably through the roof. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439409452i/15832977._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='534' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Honestly, I think I'm still processing, and trying to rid myself of some of the horrific image</span>
  <span id="freeText14740746455846841401" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 Stars...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439409452i/15832976._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I may need therapy after this damn book. For the faint of heart...it certainly is not. More than once I had to stop reading, overwhelmed, I had to remind myself certain characters weren't real, so I couldn't hunt them down and destroy them - I couldn't make them suffer, over and over... Gah. Even now, thinking about some of the stuff I read, my blood pressure is probably through the roof. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439409452i/15832977._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="534" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Honestly, I think I'm still processing, and trying to rid myself of some of the horrific images Tillie has painted in my head. At times it just felt like too much, which is way this wasn't a five star read for me, I wish it had been a little less graphic at times, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[kids being hurt, its a hard limit for me, and there were just too many incidences in this story. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That said, Flame and Maddie together were adorable, the way they come together and overcome the horrors of their past, it was truly beautiful. Their interactions have such an innocent undertone, honest and real - while my heart broke for them, the terrible things they were forced to endure, the love they have for each other made this story unforgettable. <br><br><i>
  <b>"The night is clear too. Not a cloud in the sky. And the stars and the moon have come out to watch."<br>But I didn't bother looking up. What the fuck were the stars and moon, when I had her? I couldn't take my eyes off her.</b>
</i><br><br>Special shout out to Viking and AK! Those two made my heart happy. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436447687i/15459916._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="56" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Flame's book!!!!</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438603551i/15733374._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

HERE WE GO!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2d91pbm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

It's breaking my heart reading his need to control the fire within himself..Then out come the knives!! This is heartbreakingly raw..Drip, Drip the sound of my tears falling down my cheeks, my heart is breaking for all that is flame..<br><br><b>NOW</b><br><br><i>
  <b>He has evil running through his veins. The way he behaves, the way he cuts himself. The darkness of his soul.</b>

</a><br><br><i>He didn’t ever wanna live like this. You know what he said to do if he ever went nuclear. If at any point he never came back out of his fucked up head.</i> <br><br>You ever want to jump inside a book and become one of those characters, the character that saves the day, that tries to save the broken male, the one that loves that broken man unconditionally well Flame for me is that book!! The kind of book that made me FEEL, the kind of book that BROKE my heart, FLAMES story broke me into little pieces..And that is what I love about books like this they make me feel things that on a day to day basis outside of my books I wouldn't necessarily feel..<br><br><b>A PRODUCT OF HIS CHILDHOOD</b><br><br><i>There's an evil living inside you boy. An evil I'm gonna make damn sure is exorcised. Make you normal. Make you right.</i><br><br><b>One, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight, nine, ten, eleven…</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=13zbvv5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie, Maddie...</b><br><br>I really don't want to read what his father does to him to try and make him right!! This is going to kill me!! <br><br>When we got that little glimpse of Flame in the previous book and his self mutilation and his inability to touch thinking if he touches he will hurt the recipient, I will not lie I did roll the eyes and was like here we go this guy is fucked up way beyond repair, but now we're privy to what made him the way he is, there is such depth to his character. And as I put above he is a product of his childhood, it's been manipulated in him to think the way he thinks..<br><br>With each book in this series Tillie just seems to push that darkness a little more each book, this book was darker than the others which I really really loved..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=dvhjwy" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><i>
  <b> I was seventeen...seventeen, when I embraced the darkness. Seventeen when I fucking became flame</b>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1408551256" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1408551256?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26072113-souls-unfractured">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=i-like-it-dark-and-twisted">i-like-it-dark-and-twisted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1408551256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11032044618140798251"><b>5 FLAMING Stars</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Wow! I just cleared off a spot on my Favorite Shelf for this one. To some friends’ surprise, the first book of this series didn’t wow me at all and I found the love connection to be ridiculously far-fetched and story line was a tad dare I say lame? With an open mind, I ventured into the second book of the series and even though it was a much better read, I still wasn’t drinking the Hangman Lover’s Kool-Aide. However, this third book of the series was a winner and I’ve</span>
  <span id="freeText11032044618140798251" style="display:none"><b>5 FLAMING Stars</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Wow! I just cleared off a spot on my Favorite Shelf for this one. To some friends’ surprise, the first book of this series didn’t wow me at all and I found the love connection to be ridiculously far-fetched and story line was a tad dare I say lame? With an open mind, I ventured into the second book of the series and even though it was a much better read, I still wasn’t drinking the Hangman Lover’s Kool-Aide. However, this third book of the series was a winner and I’ve happily joined the masses! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491671857i/22435556.jpg" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was completely captivated by Flame from the first few pages of the story. While Maddie is just the right percentage of broken to be able to help the scary as fuck Hangman. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Flame’s past will crush a reader and had me cringing every time the author brought me back to his childhood. His feelings for Maddie will give hope that somewhere under the disturbing acts of cutting himself right in front of your face and I can’t even discuss what he would do over that damn hatch in his cabin…yikes! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444130751ra/16457492.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However scary Flame is and his behaviors misunderstood, he does indeed have a soul and a big heart. A heart and soul that wants more than what he has been given in this life with the beautiful woman he helped rescue from a religious nightmare as scary as his own.<br><br><b>
  <i>”"I know I'm different. I know I don't see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if its the only one I'll ever understand." </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380361319ra/712292.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tillie Cole brought a couple so fractured together and made them work. Their progression to love was totally believable and their love scenes were very unique (I hung on every word).<br><br><b>
  <i>“I used to wonder how two people- one broken girl, and one broken boy- could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that’s how. They fight their way through… together.”</i>
</b><br><br>If you're like me kind of indifferent about this series, give this one a go! If you stopped at book one, give this book a go! If you have been a fan since the get go and were one of those who told me to try Flame's book (Christy &amp; Brandi) -Thank You.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11032044618140798251" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
