<div id="review_3504119242" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3504119242" />
    <a title="Tears Of Venus, but humans call me Mina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina"><img alt="Tears Of Venus, but humans call me Mina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597082036p2/58714144.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3504119242?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tears Of Venus, but humans call me Mina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tears Of Venus, but humans call me Mina" href="/user/show/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina">Tears Of Venus, but humans call me Mina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">those who seek light in the darkness</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina?shelf=loki-approves">loki-approves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina?shelf=all-the-stars">all-the-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3504119242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15607727983360111018"><blockquote>5 my babies ⭐️s</blockquote><br/><b>Song :</b> <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YhatytEAJh4' rel='nofollow noopener'> Dust To Dust</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that’s how. They fight their way through… together.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><b>My Google search history</b> <br/><i>How to kill fictional characters? <br/>How to get inside a book and what weapons can you bring?<br/>How to revive dead fictional characters to kill them again? Slowly and painfully?</i><br/><br/><b>The government agent monitoring me</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018671.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Flame</b> and <b>Maddie</b> have capture</span>
  <span id="freeText15607727983360111018" style="display:none"><blockquote>5 my babies ⭐️s</blockquote><br><b>Song :</b> <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YhatytEAJh4" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dust To Dust</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that’s how. They fight their way through… together.”</blockquote>
</b><br><b>My Google search history</b> <br><i>How to kill fictional characters? <br>How to get inside a book and what weapons can you bring?<br>How to revive dead fictional characters to kill them again? Slowly and painfully?</i><br><br><b>The government agent monitoring me</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018671.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Flame</b> and <b>Maddie</b> have captured my heart from the very first book and I’ve been dying to get to them. And now<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018672.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Story time AKA let’s talk about ✨me✨</u>
</b><br>I’m a sponge first and a human second. One of those annoying people that absorb every emotion around them until they’re saturated with it. Those who are happy when people are happy. Who are sad when people are sad. Who spend sleepless nights thinking about every injustice, every wrong miserable painful thing going on in the world. Who stop watching the news because they can’t handle what’s being reported. Whose hearts constantly bleed for all those who just need a little <b>helping hand</b>, a little <b>love</b> and some <b>compassion</b>; who just need <b>someone</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018673.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Flame’s flashbacks had me sleeping on my bathroom floor for an entire night, depleted of tears and energy. <b>Rachel</b>, I wouldn't have been able to do it without you. Thanks for being an amazing person and going through these ups and downs with me.🖤<br>Knowing this is happening to millions of children out there? <b>It kills me</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018674.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>
  <u>Maddie and Flame’s story</u>
</b><br><i>Reading this book was like walking into a war torn field. Every way you look, there is chaos, death, destruction and pain. The scene is so vivid, you can almost hear the echo of screams, smell the metallic odor of blood, see death take over and feel, feel as all hope is lost. The heavy cloying smoke surrounds you, and as you follow one of the delicate tendrils as it rises above- as if yearning to slip away from the horrors it witnessed down there- you realize that upon escaping to the vastness of the sky, it starts to depict a scene. To tell a story. You were too busy looking down at the results of a war raged between countries and nations, that you missed the one up there, fueled by the cruelty of one human towards another, on a lesser scale but no less significant. <br>As you look closer, you see thousands of scenarios playing every single horrible thing humanity is capable of. You see it all and you can’t look away. You can’t look away as the father rapes his child, as the mother ignores hers, as the innocent prisoner is directed to his death, as a person is prosecuted for his race, color and beliefs while another dies from hunger, thirst and cold.<br>The tendrils keep on ascending until they set in the sky, as if finally home. That’s when you understand that every star in the night sky is a pained soul who has left earth. The shinier the star, the more the soul has suffered. They’re there to comfort those in suffering, to light up their dark nights and tell them they’re there. They see them. They feel them. They’re looking out for them and they invite them to wish upon them. <br>The realization brings you to your knees, and that’s when you see it. Underneath the dust and debris, sprouting from the slaughtered soil, standing delicately but fiercely in shining gold and spotless white, is a daisy. What is it doing there, and how has it survived, you wonder. How can something so beautiful, so vibrant, so pure, grow in a place so dark, so stagnant, so hopeless, you ask yourself. How can such light exist in such darkness? How can such beauty exist in such ugliness? <br>Let me tell you, my friend, that daisy in the middle of a war torn field, illuminated by billions of stars is the union of two Souls Unfractured : <b>Flame</b> and his <b>Maddie</b>. </i><br><br> <b>
  <u>Flame</u>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>People said I was a fucking freak. All my life they’d told me I was born wrong.</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018675.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>“She would never want me. I’m a fucking retard. I don’t think right in here. I’m fucked up—I don’t get people, they don’t get me. And I ain’t ever gonna be able to read people. Why would someone as perfect as her want someone as fucked up as me? Someone who isn’t right in the head?”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577174256ra/28660847.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There’s nothing I hate more than hugs, but if I could find a way to get in this story, I would wrap myself around Flame and never <b>ever</b> let go. <br>The things his piece of shit sperm donor did to him and made him feel. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I held up my wrist to show him I was trying to get the flames out. That I didn’t need the church, that I could do it myself. I could get the flames out myself, if he would just let me try. But he just hit my wrist down, then struck me on the back of my head.</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>He was angry with me, again. But I didn’t understand what I’d done to make him so mad? I tried. I always tried to make him happy. But it never worked. He just got madder. He just hurt me more and more. And I felt his disappoint deep inside me. I couldn't sleep, and all the worry made my hands shake. I… I was so confused. I didn’t mean to make him mad. I tried… I really, really tried.</blockquote>
</b><br>I have never, not once in my life, hated someone with this kind of passion. I don’t care if he’s not real, I just wanna<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018676.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My baby went through so much and just going through my highlights has me sobbing again.<br><b>
  <blockquote>“The flames hurt all of the time. They wouldn’t let me release them. They left me alone in a room, tied to a bed, letting the flames burn me alive.”</blockquote>
</b><br>He thinks he’s a monster with flames of evil in his blood. It’s what he’s been told since he was a child and what he believes to be true. <br><b>
  <blockquote>No one ever wanted to stay. They always left. I was always here alone.</blockquote>
</b><br>Until his Maddie came along.<br><b>
  <blockquote>Maddie had liked something on me? No one had ever liked me.<br>She said she would care for me. No one had ever cared for me before.<br>I knew she would leave. Because everyone left. No one ever wanted me for long.</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“With her beside me, I can sleep with no demons in my head. And she sings to me. To me. No one’s ever sang to me before.”</blockquote>
</b><br>He’s so sweet, so loving, so protective even tho he thinks his touch will hurt her.<br><b>
  <blockquote>I looked at my rigid fingers. They looked just like everyone else’s, but they didn’t work the same. Because other people could touch someone else. They could’ve put their hand on her face after she’d said thank you. They could’ve felt her skin. They could’ve maybe made her feel better.<br>But then the frustration filled my heart, and I thought, Your touch is poison. You’ll hurt her.</blockquote>
</b><br>But when he realized that he can, in fact, touch her?<br><b>
  <blockquote>I didn’t want to leave her. I just wanted to be near her.<br>I fucking just needed to be close.</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>Evil still infused my body, but I could breathe. I panted. I sweated. But I could breathe. When I looked at her, I could breathe.</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Your cheeks are blushing again. That means you liked it. You told me you blushed when you liked something. That I’d just made you feel special.” His lips rubbed together, and I could see his mind turning over. “You liked sleeping next to me. Because it made you feel special.”<br>A smile crept on my lips. “Yes.”<br>“I liked it too.”</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>What the fuck were the stars and moon, when I had her?</blockquote>
</b><br>Me to him :<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018677.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And when he finally confronted his father??<br><b>
  <blockquote>“I wasn’t a fucking sinner. I was fucking different. I am fucking different. My head doesn’t work right, like others. But it wasn’t a fucking sin, I wasn’t fucking evil, I was different.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018678.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You owning that shit now?”<br>“She owns me. That’s all that fucking matters.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018679.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>
  <u>Maddie</u>
</b><br>This girl is <b>the real MVP</b>. She’s the proof that being broken doesn’t have to be who you are, your identity and your truth. You’re so much more. We’re so much more. <b>She’s so much more</b>. <br><b>
  <blockquote>For a fleeting moment I had the silly thought that if I made myself small enough, that if I pressed myself against the wall as small as I possibly could, then the Elders might leave me alone.</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote> I instantly learned to dread that room. Then after a while, it became my life. And that’s when I died inside.</blockquote>
</b><br>I don’t think I’ve ever had the pleasure of reading about such a strong character. She’s a <b>pint-sized warrior</b>, just like AK said. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I shook with white-hot anger, incandescent at being ignored. I had been ignored enough in my life, pushed aside, thought of as weak and unimportant.<br>Not now. Not today.</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1544390502ra/26720336.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>“That is the beauty of freewill, Lilah. We choose our own actions. Unlike in commune, here we get to be the masters of our fate. I will go to Flame. Whatever transpires, transpires.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1568071142ra/28124489.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>I think perhaps, if you are told something often enough, you end up believing it. But maybe, just maybe, someone comes into your life and makes you question yourself. Makes you believe you are worth something.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018680.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All she’s ever wanted was to feel safe, and with Flame, she does. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I held my right hand in the air, and with my left hand, intertwined the fingers just to imagine how it might feel.<br>A hand holding mine.<br>One simple touch.<br>A touch that said so much.</blockquote>
</b><br>I dare you to find me any hero who’s as swoon worthy as Maddie is. <br><b>
  <blockquote>You are my faith awakened.</blockquote>
</b> <br><b>
  <blockquote>“So you may think you cannot be loved. But in my heart, in my healing soul, I am begging the question, how can you not? Because for me, you are truth. My truth. My heart, is all you.” </blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I like you laughing.”<br>I sighed and whispered, “And I just love you in any fashion.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598515542ra/30021574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Their love</u>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“We are Flame and Maddie. And we have survived.”</blockquote>
</b><br>How something so pure, so beautiful, so gentle can grow between two people who have been on the receiving end of such heinous acts, I have no idea. But it gives me <b>hope</b>. <br><b>
  <blockquote> “Then what do you believe in?” he tentatively asked.<br>Smiling through my tears, I said, “You. I believe in you.” Raising my head, my nose brushed his, and I confessed, “I believe in me. In us. We are all I need. All I’ll ever need from this point on.”</blockquote>
</b><br>Usually when two people are broken, one’s healing is overshadowed by the other’s. That did not happen here. These two <b>saved each other</b>.<br><b>
  <blockquote>“But I like you touching me. You make me feel safe.”<br>“You cool my blood,” I replied.</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“For once, in my whole life, I like being me.”<br>“Because of Flame?”<br>“Mostly, yes. He has brought me to life. But through him, I feel more at peace with myself. Does that make sense?”</blockquote>
</b><br>It’s the little things. How she loves his eyes when everybody else says they’re dead and soulless. How he’s ready to follow her to the depths of his own personal hell, the church.<br><b>
  <blockquote>“Are you ready?”<br> “No,” he rasped. <br>“But will you follow me?” I prompted.<br>“Anywhere.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018681.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I don’t ever remember being happy.”<br>Fighting back tears, I whispered, “Then this is what we will hope for. Happiness... Because Flame?”<br>“What?” he pushed, voice barely registering a whisper.<br>“You are my happiness.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018682.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I know I’m different. I know I don’t see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if it’s the only one I’ll ever understand.”</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I draw, and that makes me happy. I was wondering what makes you happy?”<br>“I watch you.”<br> “That is what makes you happy? To watch me? Does it not bore you? I am asking what makes you happy? What you like doing most?”<br>Flame shook his head, then his eyes that I adored so much, met mine. “Being near you. Seeing you.”</blockquote>
</b><br>I can go on and on, but all you really need to know is that <b>he’s her Flame and she’s his Maddie</b>. I imagine them both wrapped in gold like Japanese pottery, to highlight just how beautiful and imperfectly perfect they are. 🖤 Hopefully Flame doesn’t scream as much, because I’m afraid for my boy’s vocal chords. 🥺<br><br><b>
  <u>AK and Viking</u>
</b><br>Their love for Flame and their bond was <b>everything</b>. I wish I could add quotes but I’m sure you’re cursing me by now for the long review, and GR is telling me I only have few characters left. 😭 Just know that will all my heart, <b>I love AK and Viking</b>. 🖤<br><br><b>
  <u>Mae</u>
</b><br>UGH she gets on my every nerve, going on about how much she loves and cares for her sisters. Bitch, I’ve been in your head and <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018683.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Rider/Cain</u>
</b><br>He's too stupid to live. How he survived natural selection is beyond me. I don't hate him but he's irrelevant to me LOL.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598446661ra/30018684.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And finally, a <b>breathtaking quote</b> by our pint-sized warrior queen.<br><b>
  <blockquote>“What are words? Sometimes the flick of a pair of eyes or the flush of skin reveals everything you need to know. Words can wound. Silence can heal.”</blockquote>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15607727983360111018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_997936383" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/997936383" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/997936383?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=dark-and-twisted">dark-and-twisted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=arc-drc">arc-drc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer997936383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1815980060338938863"><i>August 10th 2015 - Review now posted!</i><br/><br/><b>4.95 **<u>beautiful heartbreak</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438781660i/15753454.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We are Flame and Maddie. And we have survived”<br/>“We have found each other, and we are never letting each other go.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Flame and Maddie stole my heart.</b> But when you consider how invested I already was in both characters before I even started reading the book, falling in love with them all over again was no surprise at all. What I couldn’t have anticipated was the care and sensitivity with which Ms. Cole developed this</span>
  <span id="freeText1815980060338938863" style="display:none"><i>August 10th 2015 - Review now posted!</i><br><br><b>4.95 **<u>beautiful heartbreak</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438781660i/15753454.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We are Flame and Maddie. And we have survived”<br>“We have found each other, and we are never letting each other go.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Flame and Maddie stole my heart.</b> But when you consider how invested I already was in both characters before I even started reading the book, falling in love with them all over again was no surprise at all. What I couldn’t have anticipated was the care and sensitivity with which Ms. Cole developed this love story. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22107214-souls-unfractured" rel="nofollow noopener">Souls Unfractured</a> was the most beautiful and yet gut wrenching read I had all year. The level of emotion was so high it made me cry. It made me cry a lot. <br><br>This is the third instalment in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/128581-hades-hangmen" rel="nofollow noopener">Hades Hangmen Series</a> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Tillie Cole</a> and probably shouldn’t be read as a standalone. The main story surrounds Maddie and Flame, in and of itself a new couple, but the surrounding plots are a continuation of the first two books.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438822822i/15759592.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the first moment Maddie and Flame met in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22020052-it-ain-t-me-babe" rel="nofollow noopener">It Ain’t Me, Baby</a> and he killed her abuser, I was enthralled with their dynamic and wanted to get to know both characters and see if there is a relationship at all possible. <br><br>They don’t disappoint. Over the course of two books we witnessed Flame being batshit crazy watching over the little one and Maddie hiding behind the window looking out into the world, watching her saviour and the only man she is not afraid of - never talking or touching. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“What are words? Sometimes the flick of a pair of eyes or the flush of skin reveals everything you need to know. Words can wound. Silence can heal.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>But that dynamic changes at the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22107044-heart-recaptured" rel="nofollow noopener">Heart Recaptured</a> when Flame takes a bullet for Maddie. Once he comes back both have to face each other and maybe even come to terms with their connection.<br><br>I can’t even begin to tell you how amazing and carefully constructed the romance is in this book. Both characters are broken to a degree that they are barely able to function and in Flame’s case he is about to hit the point of no return.<br><br>As it turns out the only thing that keeps them moving is each other.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439038610i/15785800.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Flame is a tortured hero and when I say that I actually mean it. The things he went through in his life that made him the unhinged out of control self mutilating nutjob that he is today and it seriously broke my heart. Hearing about his past is not easy to take and might just be too much for some people. Ms. Cole really dives in with this one. It is graphic, mind numbing and leaves your heart in tatters.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You, Flame. My tortured boy. You gave me life and light.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The only thing that can get Flame out of this hell hole is Maddie. Now, she was a complete surprise for me. Up until this point we only got to see her as the silent girl sitting around and ignoring the world. Not an unusual thing when you consider the things she endured all her life living in the abusive cult. But to my great pleasure she actually was the anchor here. The tables are turned, whereas in the first two instalments the girls needed saving this time around Maddie is the one extending the hand. Yes, Flame and Maddie save each other, but I think it is safe to say without her resilience and devotion <i>Souls Unfractured</i> would have been half as good and they would still be watching each other through a window.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438823815i/15759699.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One thing that really stood out for me in this book was the friendship between Flame, Viking and AK - the so called ‘psycho trio’. I loved their untouchable loyalty and bond. There is nothing they wouldn’t do for each other. Really a remarkable thing. <br><br>What else is there to say? Cain is a tool, but there is light at the end of the tunnel. I hear one of the next books will be about him. Keeping my fingers crossed for him. <br><br>After reading me gushing about this book, you might wonder why there are only 4.95 stars. There was one little twist that was just unnecessary and redundant in my humble opinion. In the end it was only an eye roll moment but I really needed to put it in the rating since it bothered me nonetheless. If you scream at your kindle 'not again' something must be wrong. ;D But in the grand scheme of things it really doesn't matter.<br><br>All in all, I have to say this was my absolutely favourite couple in the series so far. The love story was so incredibly beautiful, moving and I will treasure it for a long time. The writing is on point. When you can't keep reading because of all the tears you are shedding you just know something must be right.<br><br>Thank you for the memories, Ms. Cole! <br><br><br><i>**ARC very kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438283331i/15689793.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giorgia ~ Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giorgia ~ Reads" href="/user/show/97546350-giorgia-reads">Giorgia ~ Reads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26072113-souls-unfractured">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=dark-themes">dark-themes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=2020-read">2020-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=motorcycle-club">motorcycle-club</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3343858873" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13751887551606631986"><b> 5 Stars </b> <br/><br/>If this book was just a collection of sincere conversations between Maddie and Flame, I would still give it five stars. That’s how <b>genuine and moving</b> that relationship was. <br/><br/>I have to admit I have a soft spot for scarred or broken male characters. (Zsadist from BDB anyone!?) <b>Flame represented such an antithesis. A remorseless killer with a gentle soul. A person who doesn’t get the nuance of human emotion yet is able to feel so much. </b>He broke my heart. I could see him as a child, scared,</span>
  <span id="freeText13751887551606631986" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars </b> <br /><br />If this book was just a collection of sincere conversations between Maddie and Flame, I would still give it five stars. That’s how <b>genuine and moving</b> that relationship was. <br /><br />I have to admit I have a soft spot for scarred or broken male characters. (Zsadist from BDB anyone!?) <b>Flame represented such an antithesis. A remorseless killer with a gentle soul. A person who doesn’t get the nuance of human emotion yet is able to feel so much. </b>He broke my heart. I could see him as a child, scared, misunderstood and so, so lonely. I’ve never wanted to see a character get a HEA more than Flame. <br /><br />Maddie was his other half. If there ever was a couple to fit together so perfectly, to balance each other out and to understand each other, they are it! <b>When they were together, even when they were having the most inconsequential conversation, there was a sense of peace and gentleness surrounding them</b>. I just loved it! <br /><br />Also, I can’t help but notice the contrast between how pure their relationship was and the background on which it developed, (The MC, The Order) it only made it stand out more. <br /><br />And can we talk about the book cover?! I can practically see them in that picture. This series has some of <b>the best, fitting and most heartbreaking covers. </b><br /><br />When it comes to the plot of the book, I feel like it’s<b> less action packed and more character driven</b> and I was fine with that. Both Flame and Maddie were complex and interesting as people so I could read 1000 pages about them and not get bored. <br /><br />TW: There’s a lot of dark content. Both Maddie and Flame’s pasts are not easy to read about. A lot of talk about child abuse.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8126135137699362921"><b>5 "Let it shine" STARS</b><br/><br/><i>For fractured souls are like magnets.<br/>Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss…"</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/image.jpg1_zpsjqvow74w.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438954498i/15774022._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image.jpg1_zpsjqvow74w.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Every single expectation was met and exceeded. Even a few hopes and dreams were granted in this breathtaking and heart wrenching story and series!!! <br/><br/>If you're a fan of the Hades Hangmen and Tillie Cole, like me, you've been anxiously awaiting Flame and Maddie's story. I won't give too much away because this story must truly be experienced to fully appreciate and capture all the wonder and aw</span>
  <span id="freeText8126135137699362921" style="display:none"><b>5 "Let it shine" STARS</b><br><br><i>For fractured souls are like magnets.<br>Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss…"</i><br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/image.jpg1_zpsjqvow74w.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438954498i/15774022._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zpsjqvow74w.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Every single expectation was met and exceeded. Even a few hopes and dreams were granted in this breathtaking and heart wrenching story and series!!! <br><br>If you're a fan of the Hades Hangmen and Tillie Cole, like me, you've been anxiously awaiting Flame and Maddie's story. I won't give too much away because this story must truly be experienced to fully appreciate and capture all the wonder and awe of Tillie Cole.<br><br><b>Here's my 11 thoughts or favourite quotes:</b><br><br><b>1. Flame: <i>"He had midnight eyes. Was pierced. Tattooed. Strong. And filled with pure rage. But he was mine. And when he was mine, he was gentle, caring and just as broken as I was.</i></b> <br><br>His story was dark, filled with anguish, rage and utter heartbreak. <br><br><b>"My skin felt on fire. My soul felt on fire."</b><br><a href="http://imgur.com/85MThtt" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439054256ra/15789111.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>2. Maddie: <i>"A fucking pint-sized warrior." <br><br>"My heart was dark and empty without her. And nothing I could do would take it away."</i></b><br><br>The youngest of the three sisters and also the most brutally damaged by the Order. Yet also the bravest and the strongest in so many ways. <br><br><b>3.</b> Didn't think it was possible to love Flame, AK and Vike any more than I did going into this story but these guys... <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/PTrio_zps1y5236xp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439050899i/15788363._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo PTrio_zps1y5236xp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4.</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Flame_zps8uqzjfjn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438954498i/15774021.jpg" alt=" photo Flame_zps8uqzjfjn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>5.<br><br><i>“What are words? Sometimes the flick of a pair of eyes or the flush of skin reveals everything you need to know. Words can wound. Silence can heal.”</i></b><br><br><b>6.</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/flame%20quote_zpspha4ctg5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>7. <br><br><i>"I used to wonder how two people - one broken girl, and one broken boy - could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that's how. They fight their way through...together."</i></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/WaqlsGL" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>9. The Hades Hangmen: Loved catching up with Styx and Mae, Ky and Lilah and learning more about the men and their club. I'd ride with these warriors any day. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/dmXeN7Z" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435108932ra/15303921.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>10. My words won't adequately capture all the emotions I felt when reading this tortured, dark and also light and beautiful story. For all the pain and chilling numbness...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/6YUGVEW" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439054256ra/15789110.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>...there was also salvation and freedom.<br><br>11. Finally, Tillie Cole, thank you for such a breathtakingly beautiful story and for the Hades Hangmen...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Ef7ydoY" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1010933198?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=2015-favorite">2015-favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=abused">abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=barely-made-it-through">barely-made-it-through</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-leading-lady">best-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=beautiful-cover">beautiful-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=my-heart-can-barely-take-it">my-heart-can-barely-take-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=dark-and-gritty">dark-and-gritty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1010933198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9501344542864394927"><b>~5 LOVING Flame and Maddie STARS~</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441173501i/16074017.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>"For fractured souls are like magnets. Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss."</b><br/><br/>Souls Unfractured is the long awaited third book in the Hades Hangmen. The entire series is centered around three sisters and their escape from a cult. They have found a safe haven in the Hades Hangmen MC! In the previous books, we witnessed Mae and Lilah find happiness with their motorcycle men and now it is time for the youngest sister Maddie to find her piece of happiness. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441230902i/16080479.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>"The</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9501344542864394927" style="display:none"><b>~5 LOVING Flame and Maddie STARS~</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441173501i/16074017.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"For fractured souls are like magnets. Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss."</b><br><br>Souls Unfractured is the long awaited third book in the Hades Hangmen. The entire series is centered around three sisters and their escape from a cult. They have found a safe haven in the Hades Hangmen MC! In the previous books, we witnessed Mae and Lilah find happiness with their motorcycle men and now it is time for the youngest sister Maddie to find her piece of happiness. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441230902i/16080479.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"The flames never calmed. They forever f*cking burned. But with her...I wanted to grip her tighter. I wanted to hold her closer."-Flame</b><br><br>From the moment that Maddie was rescued from the horrific world of the cult she had her heart and soul bound to one man. FLAME! Flame is a mystery. He keeps to himself and is different from the other men in the club. Flame has demons that cause him great pain. He finds relief for his pain by cutting himself. He is afraid to touch anyone because he believes he is toxic. And yet, somehow Maddie has captured his heart. Even if he doesn't quite now how to express himself, there is one thing he knows, Maddie is his! <br><br><b>"Because she was mine."-Flame</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298314ra/682410.gif" width="400" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Flame has found solace just being near Maddie. He won't touch her but he can't stay away. Maddie is equally damaged by the atrocities she has faced from her life in the cult. However, being near Flame has given her hope for a better life. Could there ever be a future between the two?<br><br><b>"He was still the man who protected me. He was still the silent shadow that kept me safe."-Maddie</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425312533ra/13875360.gif" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As Flame and Maddie find away to be together their past demons surface. Individually they are both sick and broken souls and yet, together they seem to find a way. It is a painful journey stifled by dirty memories that will cause your heart to ache and your stomach to churn. And yet, the tender moments where peace is discovered will fill your heart to the brim with love. Additionally, for me, the sexy scenes were even more sexy because truthfully the anticipation of these two coming together was so worth the wait! There is a a great deal of love blooming between the two as the plot develops. And when they finally come together, it is explosive and so beautiful. The dual POV really offers the full spectrum of the story and the tempo was consistently steady with dueling moments of intensity and sweet moments of relief. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441230902i/16080481.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall, I can honestly say everything about this read was captivating! The characters are complex and thoroughly developed by the author. Each individual story line continues to flourish as the books progress. I have been anticipating Flame and Maddie's story from the moment I finished the first book and thankfully Ms. Cole certainly did not disappoint. As par for the course, for me, she delivers every time! I think it's critical to prepare my tenderhearted GR friends. Flame and Maddie's story isn't an easy one to get through. If you like gritty romance stories, then this is the read for you. In order to experience the full arc of the story, you should start by reading the first book! I promise, you will be so glad that you invested in these characters. Thank you Ms. Cole for giving us such a magnificent love story between two broken people. It serves as a reminder that it is never too late to find love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441235354i/16081114.jpg" width="400" height="75" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We are never so broken that we cannot find a way to heal. It is never wrong to be the person you were created to be. We are all worthy of more than we ever wished or hoped for! This is one story I will never forget! <br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://craziesrusbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

<div id="review_966584293" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/966584293" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/966584293?book_show_action=true">Jun 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer966584293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9112140104752197644"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439039694i/15786068._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> 5++ Stars </b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Flame’s different. But it don’t make him any less fucking important.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>And…</b>..this is how it’s done! Souls Unfractured was everything we were anticipating, in fact it was more. It went beyond our wildest expectations, needs and wants for two characters who stole our hearts right from the beginning of this series; Flame & Maddie.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I know I’m different. I know I don’t see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if it’s the only one I’ll ever und</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText9112140104752197644" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439039694i/15786068._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 5++ Stars </b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Flame’s different. But it don’t make him any less fucking important.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>And…</b>..this is how it’s done! Souls Unfractured was everything we were anticipating, in fact it was more. It went beyond our wildest expectations, needs and wants for two characters who stole our hearts right from the beginning of this series; Flame &amp; Maddie.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I know I’m different. I know I don’t see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if it’s the only one I’ll ever understand.”</i>
</b><br><br>Souls Unfractured felt complete.<b> Complete.</b> Tillie Cole is an astounding writer. She literally involves every single one of your senses and pushes every single button demanding your attention. Her words bleeds from the pages into your heart. Her characters <b>steal </b>your heart. <b>All of them.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“…for me, you are truth. My truth. My heart, is all you.”</i>
</b><br><br>What is so incredibly flawless is her attention to detail and tying up every single question, action, behaviour and storyline without it being superfluous, contrived or complicated, or even left wanting. We are in awe of this Author and give kudos to the obvious extensive research she compiles to stay true to her story and characters.<br><br>Every single character has a voice, a heart and a purpose. The love, the brotherhood, the respect and the unity. The compassion. Tillie Cole knows when to give and when to pull back so there’s no question as to why she’s one of our all-time favourite Authors.<br><br><b>‘Two fractured souls made whole only by the other’s unconditional love.’</b><br><br>Now, Flame and Maddie’s story is not for the faint-hearted. It’s as dark, terrifying – gruesome even. Therefore, embark on this journey knowing that you will be shocked, your limits will be pushed and <b>your heart will be violently torn into bloody pieces.</b> However; like a phoenix rising out of the ashes so does the incredibly intense beauty rise out of the monstrous in Souls Unfractured. And it truly is a sight to behold. It’s pretty bloody fantastic and satisfying to a reader’s soul. In amidst the inhumane you experience striking gentle moments of belonging, healing and ultimately love.<br><br><b>‘I…I wanted him as my own. In this moment, seeing the man who had become the center of my world, breaking, I wanted nothing more than to save him. To gift him the peace he so richly deserved, even if it meant sacrificing my newly-awakened heart in the process.’</b><br><br>Let’s begin with Maddie; the sweet and fragile elf like character who’s had to endure unspeakable tragedy, horrific childhood memories and like Flame lived a nightmare whilst fully awake. Such evil is unfathomable yet at no time was it sensationalised or added for drama’s sake. Our hearts bled; our nerves were fraught as this beautiful broken soul connected to another’s – embracing, loving and uniting with its own kind – Flame.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I don’t feel the flames when you’re near. Somehow you calm the flames.”</i>
</b><br><br>Flame was not <i>simply</i> broken nor was he <i>just</i> traumatized. Those words do him no justice. He was the innocent victim of evil, a severely misunderstood boy who suffered a life stripped of everything good and loving in the world. He was neglected of a soft touch and the warm comfort that should be a natural right not a privilege. He was conditioned by other’s depravity, his gentle soul was used, abused and treated like a vessel in the most debauched manner under a misguided and self-serving justice. As Flame’s blood dripped from the self-inflicted cutting so did our tears onto the pages of our kindles.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’ll try harder to remove the flames. I’ll try harder…I…I love you.”</i>
</b><br><br>How many tears can you cry? How much can your heart truly hurt? How can the number 11 inflict such pain on your soul? How can every simple act of love and friendship shine like a beacon to neutralise all the evil, all the hurt? Well, Souls Unfractured can answer all of the questions and sets the bar so amazingly high.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I am darkness. I am pain. I am motherfucking death.”</i>
</b><br><br>Souls Unfractured was Flame and Maddie. Flame and his Maddie. Maddie and her Flame. It was <b>their</b> journey from their individual beginnings –<b> it was their story.</b> Every minute was primarily spent with them which is what made it unique, compelling, intense and so extraordinarily personal. When someone mentions ‘no frills’ you immediately think of a cheap imitation. <b>Well, not in this case.</b> In this case <i>‘no frills’</i> is the highest of accolades as we dealt with the most basic human emotion of the rawest and most natural kind. When you strip layer after layer and get to the core and this core overwhelms you as it is like no other, and shines more brightly than the <i>‘frills’</i> in which it is wrapped. That is what ultimately makes up flawlessness and originality. That is what makes us Tillie Cole. That is how you can tell something is so very special and written in blood, through sweat and tears. And believe us; there were tears of unmeasurable magnitude.<br><br><b>‘My Maddie. Her Flame.’</b><br><br> <i>**Reviewed from an ARC Copy provided by the author, with thanks.**</i><br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439039694i/15786069.png" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>**<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2014/04/28/it-aint-me-babe-by-tillie-cole/" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review for It Ain't Me Babe</a><br><br>**<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2014/12/14/heart-recaptured-hades-hangemen-2-by-tillie-cole/" rel="nofollow noopener">Our Review for Heart Recaptured</a></b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>✦✦✦ TB Blog :<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦✦✦ Come say Hi : <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦✦✦Follow us: <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦✦✦Check out: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a><br>✦✦✦ We're on TSU: <a href="https://www.tsu.co/TBBLOG" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on TSU</a></b></span>

    <a title="mel ☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41864935-mel"><img alt="mel ☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605046766p2/41864935.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1777939229?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="mel ☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="mel ☽" href="/user/show/41864935-mel">mel ☽</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26072113-souls-unfractured">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=favorite-heroes">favorite-heroes</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=mc">mc</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1777939229" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16094700456620791678"><b>reread (mar 2020)</b> — 4.75 stars<br/><br/><i>MADDIE AND FLAME ARE BOTH PRECIOUS AND MUST BE PROTECTED AT ALL COSTS.</i><br/><br/>this book is the very definition of a paradox since its so dark that i had to take a break from the series <i>for a year</i> but <u>the romance is one of the purest, most innocent thing i've ever read</u>. and every time there's a cute moment between all the dark ones, i just<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488819992ra/22156392.gif' width='350' height='210' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>i can't handle the cuteness OK? and from the very first book when Flame killed Maddie's rapist and she hugged him (when Flame doesn't like</span>
  <span id="freeText16094700456620791678" style="display:none"><b>reread (mar 2020)</b> — 4.75 stars<br><br><i>MADDIE AND FLAME ARE BOTH PRECIOUS AND MUST BE PROTECTED AT ALL COSTS.</i><br><br>this book is the very definition of a paradox since its so dark that i had to take a break from the series <i>for a year</i> but <u>the romance is one of the purest, most innocent thing i've ever read</u>. and every time there's a cute moment between all the dark ones, i just<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488819992ra/22156392.gif" width="350" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>i can't handle the cuteness OK? and from the very first book when Flame killed Maddie's rapist and she hugged him (when Flame doesn't like to be touched), i just knew their romance was gonna be so good and i was right. why? because of their emotional connection that the first 2 books failed to accomplish. <br><br>i was a little iffy with Flame since in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1777938468?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">it ain't me babe</a> he, uh, (<b>tw!</b>) <u>cut himself and was aroused whenever he did it</u>(<b>!</b>). so i didn't really know what to think of his character but ever since he met Maddie, i just loved seeing Flame being so protective to her in a very extreme way since he guards her door or stands below her window all day and night and he would always growl or go bat shit crazy whenever Maddie isn't around. <br><br>but when i discovered what Flame went through his entire childhood and what his "father" did to him to make him the way he is? i don't really know what to feel since i was both heartbroken and disgusted. it was just so disturbing so <b>for those who want to be warned first and want to read this in the future</b>, i'll explain some of it since it is <u>VERY TRIGGERING</u>.<br><blockquote>(<b>tw: spoilers</b>) Flame has autism and his whole entire childhood, his dad raped, abused, cut him, locked him in a cellar every night. he also witnessed his baby brother dying in his arms, which made him believe whatever the crazy "church" people and his dad told him where his blood is evil just because he was different. <br><br>and now, as an adult, he cuts himself and touches himself to make the "flames in his blood go away" so he has to do his painful ritual every night because the voice of his father is still in his head. he does this so won't hurt others, especially Maddie. <u>there are a few explicit scenes where nothing is held back so be warned people</u>!! </blockquote><br>i just couldn't handle the darkness of this book sometimes so im surprised i pulled through this <i>twice</i>.<br><br>Flame and Jamie from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10964.Outlander__Outlander___1_" title="Outlander (Outlander, #1) by Diana Gabaldon" rel="nofollow noopener">outlander</a> are honestly the characters i know that have suffered the most in EVERY platform.<br><br>but anyways, i love how Maddie and Flame are each others' salvation. their relationship is just so precious and wholesome. they're both protective of one another and i love how Flame turns into a shy softie whenever Maddie is around. it just made me feel some type of way, because i mean, their convo would be like this, <br><blockquote>
  <b>"I draw, and that makes me happy. I was wondering what makes you happy?"<br>I watched Flame's face as his eyes flitted from side to side, when he said, "I watch you."<br>Heat infused my body, and I whispered, "That is what makes you happy? To watch me? Does it not bore you? I am asking what makes <i>you</i> happy? What you like doing the most?<br>Flame shook his head, then his eyes that I adored so much, met mine. "Being near you. Seeing you."</b>
</blockquote><br>UGH MY HEART. i just can't handle the cuteness it's just too much. and when they finally touched and kissed for the first time and Flame was in so much awe because his "evil blood" didn't hurt her?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439246972ra/15813352.gif" width="350" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and y'all know how the H usually says all the swoony things? well here, Maddie is the swoony one because everything she says to Flame makes ME fall in love with HER. honestly, Flame deserves all the love Maddie gives him and im all for that.<br><br>this book is my definite favorite right now because of the wholesome content of Maddie and Flame's relationship but it's definitely one of the darkest in the series so far so <u>PEOPLE, ONLY READ THIS SERIES IF YOU'RE IN THE RIGHT MINDSET BECAUSE THIS IS VERY TRIGGERING</u>.<br><br>only reason why i downgraded my rating just a lil bit is because the <b>bad guys here always die so quickly</b>!! like, pls. just— just <i>no</i>. <br><br>pardon my language here but fuck that Judah character, that little pedophile bitchass. im sorry, im just so angry with him he is literally the worst character i've ever read about in a long time. but anyways, i can't wait to read Rider's book cuz i love a good ole bad guy turned good redemption story and i can't wait for Judah's death. <br><br>* * * <br><b>original rating</b> — 5 stars</span>

<div id="review_1158015168" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1158015168" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1158015168?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1158015168" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10789574568598753849">LIVE EARLY!- AMZ- <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1IEhoOD'>http://amzn.to/1IEhoOD</a><br/><br/><b>4.25 "Unlikely Saviors" Stars!<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-08/FFF766DF-4C39-4F16-9A5B-3409BA38CDEC_zpsjwhu2twh.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439063280ra/15790914.gif' alt=' photo FFF766DF-4C39-4F16-9A5B-3409BA38CDEC_zpsjwhu2twh.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Souls Unfractured</b> is one of those books that come along and I have to push myself to read it because I know it's going to stretch some of my limits. It's going to make me cringe, make me question the sanity of the human population, and it's going to stay with me well past the end...<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I'll be 100% open and say I didn't think I could finish this book. Why? For the same reason I couldn't finish book two...the sheer rawness of the s</span>
  <span id="freeText10789574568598753849" style="display:none">LIVE EARLY!- AMZ- <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1IEhoOD">http://amzn.to/1IEhoOD</a><br><br><b>4.25 "Unlikely Saviors" Stars!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-08/FFF766DF-4C39-4F16-9A5B-3409BA38CDEC_zpsjwhu2twh.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439063280ra/15790914.gif" alt=" photo FFF766DF-4C39-4F16-9A5B-3409BA38CDEC_zpsjwhu2twh.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><br>Souls Unfractured</b> is one of those books that come along and I have to push myself to read it because I know it's going to stretch some of my limits. It's going to make me cringe, make me question the sanity of the human population, and it's going to stay with me well past the end...<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I'll be 100% open and say I didn't think I could finish this book. Why? For the same reason I couldn't finish book two...the sheer rawness of the story felt like my chest was being cracked open and I felt utterly fileted (pun NOT intended). I've came to the conclusion that the blame isn't all in the subject matter of these books, it's in the ability of Ms <b>Tillie Cole </b>to create a scene so visually clear, you as the reader feel as though you have a front row center seat- a front row visual to things I really didn't fathom being able to watch. Something about these religious cults' sexual, almost sadistic rituals really disturb me, coupled with what they do to children? It's honestly too much for me at times. And I cannot <i>fathom </i>that this is going on in our world today. But I KNEW I had to read this book. I had to find answers to why <b>Flame </b>was the sick, twisted killer that he was in books 1 &amp; 2. The knife-killer that stands guard day and night below Maddie's window protecting her. The killer that can't be touched, not physically. But <b>Maddie </b>sure <i>touched </i>him...<br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>No one would ever hurt her again. If they did, they would die. <br> Die under my motherfucking blades… <br>Because she was mine. The little black-haired bitch called Maddie was mine.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>Such a Casanova...and I loved him. But, rest assured, Flame is bar-none THE most tortured hero I've ever experienced. My heart bled for that man. Yes, he's so so mentally scarred and borderline demonic in his rage at times, but, Lord did I want to hug all the pain away from that <s>sweet</s> man. But his focus was on Maddy, Mae's tiny little sister that too has endured her fair share of torture for her young years. She's very meek and too cannot stomach the touch from a man, has never <i>wanted</i> to, until Flame. So imperfect yet perfect for each other... <br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "I know I'm different. I know I don't see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if it's the only one I'll understand."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><br><br>I'm not going into a great deal on the plot line here. I'd highly recommend reading the series in order as it creates a background to the first connection Flame and Maddie experienced. The sadistic killed turns I to Maddie's hero on more than one occasion in the first two books and that stirs a sense of trust from Maddie that seems odd but so very genuine. <br><br><br>I can't begin to depict the gradual connection between these two characters. It was gut-wrenching. Through this early mutual trust, each protagonist fathers the courage to admit their weaknesses...to fight their demons. THIS part of the book was hardest for me. They had to revisit the ugly to get to the other side...together. <br><br><br>Anyone who has read this series will be promised a continued dose of <b>Hades Hangmen </b>brother loyalty, cameos from past MCs such as Styx/Mae and Ky/Lilah. We get grit and we get the ugliness that is the Christian cult the girls came from. What we get tenfold is an overwhelming sense of angsty build between both MCs. A slowly-progressed physical and emotional connection that has defied their awful circumstances. Nobody understands it but them...they are each other's <i>saviors. </i><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-08/CC13DBC1-ECC9-46E6-A9F1-C1A6D649B344_zps2fb06wf2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439063280i/15790915._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo CC13DBC1-ECC9-46E6-A9F1-C1A6D649B344_zps2fb06wf2.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I'm so glad I pushed through the scenes that are depicted so clearly in this book. Without seeing that dark, I don't think I could quite grasp the light that shines within these two when they combine their strengths to fight each other's demons. <br><br><br>I commend <b>Tillie Cole </b>for taking this seasoned dark reader and pushing my limits to the near breaking point, yet, springing me back with such a perfect love story in the end. Two very very imperfect people so perfect for each other. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-08/4C7239DF-2FA8-4619-81AA-1686E42F3899_zpsed54bnby.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439063280i/15790916._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4C7239DF-2FA8-4619-81AA-1686E42F3899_zpsed54bnby.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Looking forward to more within the <b>Hades Hangmen Series.</b> It appears at this time, 7 total books are to be written. I'd love to see Viking and AK each get a book after finding out the great guys they truly are. Friends that, no matter how flawed you are, see you for the person you truly are, including your flaws, and love you all the same! Off to finish Ky and Lilah's book now that I've donned my big-girl panties!<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Advanced copy received by author in exchange for my honest review. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433775460i/15140880.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/readingescapade" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10789574568598753849" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Maayan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13323856-maayan"><img alt="Maayan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576662192p2/13323856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1361956472?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maayan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maayan" href="/user/show/13323856-maayan">Maayan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=my-favorite-books">my-favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=disability">disability</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=safety-gang-safe">safety-gang-safe</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=has-a-playlist">has-a-playlist</a>,
