        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1361956472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4519258584397965266"><b>
  <i>"For fractured souls are like magnets.<br/>Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss…"</i>
</b><br/><br/>I LOVED this book. It was so good. When I finished reading it, all I could feel was warm and fuzzy ...<br/><br/>Flame wasn't a usual Hero. He was a mix of violent, quiet and innocent. There was something different about him… He didn't communicate like normal people. He found it hard to understand people emotions and facial expressions. He found it hard to talk to others, and more importantly - He couldn't be touched by an</span>
  <span id="freeText4519258584397965266" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"For fractured souls are like magnets.<br>Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss…"</i>
</b><br><br>I LOVED this book. It was so good. When I finished reading it, all I could feel was warm and fuzzy ...<br><br>Flame wasn't a usual Hero. He was a mix of violent, quiet and innocent. There was something different about him… He didn't communicate like normal people. He found it hard to understand people emotions and facial expressions. He found it hard to talk to others, and more importantly - He couldn't be touched by anyone. Not women... Not his brothers whom he trusts with his life. Not anyone.<br><br>Until Maddie.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439627769i/15863196._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know... Together, that’s how. They fight their way through together."<br>- Maddie </i>
</b><br><br>This little one was one of the strongest heroines I had the pleasure to read about. She went through HELL AND BACK and she survived. Not only she survived, she tried to move on with her life, and in the process she set Flame free. Free from his broken past. Free from his demons. Free from the Flames that burned him alive.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439627769i/15863197._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I know I’m different. I know I don’t see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if it’s the only one I’ll ever understand."<br>- Flame </i>
</b><br><br>Sometimes, when I'm reading a book, I just LOVE to read about two characters, dealing with what life throws at them - Together. This is what I got while reading this book. Two broken people finding each other in the middle of their broken lives and together, concurs it all. I loved to see how Maddie was the ONLY one who could get through to this scary H. I loved how she was the ONLY woman he ever touched (and ever will). I loved it how from the moment they met, he made her feel SAFE. He protected her and watched over her. Even when she didn't realized that, she was HIS from the start. Same as he was HERS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439627769i/15863198._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was truly amazing. I didn't read the previous books and if I'm being honest? I didn't felt lost. All I cared about was the romance and I got plenty of it. It was one of this 'quiet' books who focused on the romance and characters build and it worked just fine to me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437102929ra/15538612.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Safety Gang: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The book was completely safe. No OW/OM. No pushing away on either side. No separations. Flame - He was raped when he was younger by his SICK ASS FATHER. He was a virgin and never touched a woman. The heroine was his first in everything. Maddie - She was raped and sexually abused by the cult where she grew up in. The hero saved her and from that day on, she was free.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1137279445" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16350026303488657900"> "We are Flame and Maddie. And We have survived."<br/><br/>6+ EPIC STARS!!!!!!!<br/><br/>As an avid reader it seems like it is getting harder for me to be truly touched heart and soul by what I read anymore. Tillie Cole has managed to reach inside of me and take a hold of my heart and make it pump to a different beat!!! I am in utter awe right now of this author's raw talent that she has exhibited with this gut wrenching story of Flame and Maddie. I can't imagine what she went through while writing this story, as I</span>
  <span id="freeText16350026303488657900" style="display:none"> "We are Flame and Maddie. And We have survived."<br /><br />6+ EPIC STARS!!!!!!!<br /><br />As an avid reader it seems like it is getting harder for me to be truly touched heart and soul by what I read anymore. Tillie Cole has managed to reach inside of me and take a hold of my heart and make it pump to a different beat!!! I am in utter awe right now of this author's raw talent that she has exhibited with this gut wrenching story of Flame and Maddie. I can't imagine what she went through while writing this story, as I know just what kind of soul crushing pain I felt while reading it. At times it was very daunting and I didn't know if I would be able to finish it. My heart quite literally bled from the horrors that this beautiful couple went through. I have to say though that if it wasn't for the extreme traumatic and graphic scenes that we experienced through the eyes of Flame and Maddie; we probably wouldn't have felt the utter beauty of what developed between the two of them as their relationship blossomed. Having experienced such horrific lows, it made me cherish the unbreakable bond between these two characters all the more clearer. Tillie Cole brought Flame and Maddie to life in my soul, and they have made a home there for all time...I won't ever forget them. I felt every single pain and agony that they did as if I were the one living it. That is the talent of Ms. Cole; she is able to put you into a scene as if you were living and breathing it all on your own.<br /><br />As far as Flame goes, I have only ever read about one other character that comes close to how tormented he was of his past. In fact, Flame and Maddie often made me think of Zsadist and Bella, who were another couple in book land who had experienced horrors that go beyond what anyone else has experienced. (and yes, I speak as if these characters are alive; because in my heart and soul they were brought to life by the talented authors who created them!) What I loved about Flame is that he had such a tough exterior on the outside; but when Maddie was finally able to get closer to learning who he really was..he had such an innocent and naïve quality to him. He doesn't think like a "normal" person, but that just made his quirks stand out even more to me. His gentleness when it came to His Maddie was just so heartwarming. I loved the scenes of them together. They were both such tortured souls who were never shown love, and yet they loved deeper than anyone else ever did. The way that Flame protected Maddie melted me as well, and while most people might say they didn't have a "healthy" relationship; I never cared...It was more than special because it is what worked for them, and them alone. No one else could understand it but the two people who were halves of each other.<br /><br />Maddie impressed me so much through this story. She really came into her own. She had been so scared of life that she was known to watch it from the side lines..or I should say through the window looking down at everyone..Eventually though, she grabbed life by the balls and didn't let go. She was determined to make her own happiness with Her Flame and she went full speed ahead no matter how scare she was. I loved how she never once tried to change Flame. She accepted him for who he is, all of it..The good and then the really really bad. There is one part in the book where she came through for him in a way that I honestly hadn't thought she would have the strength to do, and from that point on she had my utmost respect.<br /><br />Most readers are going to ask, "is this a hard book to read." You had better believe it is. Even though it is raw and gritty, and at times beyond horrific; it is one of those books that NEEDS to be read. Seriously, it will touch your soul. There will be no forgetting it...EVER. I am not going to lie; there are some very hard to read topics in this book. Tillie Cole has pressed the envelope in this story and she went full speed ahead and spared no gruesome detail. There were times I felt physically ill, and had to stop to take a break. But the parts that I will cherish always are between Flame and Maddie, and it made all of the horrors worth enduring, just for a glimpse of their pure love. I highly recommend this book. Actually, this series as a whole is just awesome; but this book goes way beyond what most books can ever achieve. <br /><br />Tillie Cole: you are a Goddess in my eyes! You have impressed me so much with what you delivered, and I can't wait to see what you bring to the table next. You are so talented and please don't ever stop writing. It is so hard to find books now a days that touch so many people...Finding an author who has created an epic book is rare..and you my dear are a diamond in the rough, and you belong up there with the best of the best! Thank you for touching my soul, and for giving us Flame and Maddie.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16350026303488657900" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1355991164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8260123323873086127"><b>RATING: 5++++ Let it Shine Hearts!!! <3 :D</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“For fractured souls are like magnets. Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss...”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><i>Souls Unfractured</i> might not be as entrenched in the religious cult aspect as the previous two books, but it is no less emotional, heartbreaking or brutal; giving us a tale that wholeheartedly embodies the very definition of ‘love conquers all’.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “What are words? Sometimes the flick of a pair of eyes or the flush of skin reveals everything you need to kn</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8260123323873086127" style="display:none"><b>RATING: 5++++ Let it Shine Hearts!!! &lt;3 :D</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“For fractured souls are like magnets. Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss...”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>Souls Unfractured</i> might not be as entrenched in the religious cult aspect as the previous two books, but it is no less emotional, heartbreaking or brutal; giving us a tale that wholeheartedly embodies the very definition of ‘love conquers all’.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “What are words? Sometimes the flick of a pair of eyes or the flush of skin reveals everything you need to know. Words can wound. Silence can heal.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Flame and Maddie are tortured characters having gone through immense horror and suffering in their pasts, and as their story is harshly detailed for us in black and white, we experience their every emotion along with them—their longing for one another yet not being able to capitulate as well as the constant fears that manipulate their every move. As the story unfolds, both try to overcome their weaknesses and we can’t help but feel proud of their strength and willingness and joy to see two stunning characters get the happiness they deserve.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I never thought of myself as a strong person. But it is amazing how much strength you discover you have deep inside, when someone you love depends on you to be their rock, when they find themselves weak. How much courage you can muster, when the one you love relies on you to keep him from falling to the ground. And how much happiness can be harbored within your soul, when you allow someone into your heart.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Despite their inability to engage in anything physical, both Maddie and Flame are everything we could want in a devoted couple, both of them acting as balm to each other’s turbulent souls, granting each other absolution and bestowing on each other all the love they’ve denied themselves. The two of them together are enthralling from first to last page, their relationship – physical and emotional – dovetailing beautifully with the darker themes. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever more on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that’s how. They fight their way through...together.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, <i>Souls Unfractured</i> is a beautiful and utterly heart-aching story, leaving indelible marks on the soft flesh of our hearts, but also healing our frayed emotions as our two magnificent characters find peace at last. This story made me cry, the characters burrowed themselves into my heart and mind, and I just simply loved this.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> My wife quietly sang as I stared at my favourite sketch.<br>At us.<br>My Maddie.<br>Her Flame. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br><u>Other Fave Quotes:</u><br><br><b>
  <i> “I am darkness. I am pain. I am motherfucking death.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i> “I love you, Flame. And I will spend the rest of my life trying to make you believe that you are worthy of being loved.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i> “You are my miracle, Flame Cade. You truly are my soul’s other half.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i> “I know I’m different. I know I don’t see the world like everyone else does. But I want to see your world, Maddie. Even if it’s the only one I’ll ever understand.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i> “You, Flame. My Flame. My tortured boy. You gave me life and light.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i> I used to dream that I was a butterfly. That I would spread my colorful wings and fly away from all the pain. But now, when Flame was near, I dreamed anew. I dreamed that one day I would know what his hand felt like holding mine. </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i> “I sometimes imagine what our hands would look like...touching. What they would look like with out fingers intertwined. I wonder if it would make me smile. At times I daydream that it would be something we could do.” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468111482i/19668082._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Posted: July 9, 2016</b>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1094180171" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6583926142442561073"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435532002i/15356983.jpg' width='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> Souls Unfractured <br/><b>Series:</b> Hades Hangmen, #3<br/><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release date: </b> 11th August, 2015<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438767569i/15750969._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>”How can you be evil when you ignite such hope in me?”</b><br/><br/>If like me you are a follower and fan of Tillie Cole’s Hades Hangmen series, there isn’t a shadow of a doubt as to much you’ve been eagerly anticipating Flame and Maddie’s book. My enjoyment of the series has grown with each Club member but the prospect of being inside Flames’s head had</span>
  <span id="freeText6583926142442561073" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435532002i/15356983.jpg" width="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> Souls Unfractured <br><b>Series:</b> Hades Hangmen, #3<br><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br><b>Release date: </b> 11th August, 2015<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438767569i/15750969._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>”How can you be evil when you ignite such hope in me?”</b><br><br>If like me you are a follower and fan of Tillie Cole’s Hades Hangmen series, there isn’t a shadow of a doubt as to much you’ve been eagerly anticipating Flame and Maddie’s book. My enjoyment of the series has grown with each Club member but the prospect of being inside Flames’s head had my curiosity at an all time high.<br><br><b>”You, Flame. My Flame. My tortured boy. You gave me life and light."</b><br><br>Through previous mentions of Flame, I’d have easily described him as unstable, volatile and menacing. However, in true Tillie Cole fashion, she tells his story with such heart and vigour it’s impossible to not want to climb into the pages and embrace this misunderstood and fragile man. His story is dark, darker than I anticipated and his light comes in the guise of Maddie. <br><br><b>“You saved me. You protected me. You sat outside my door, day and night, to make sure I was safe. You paced before my window each night.”</b><br><br>Maddie is the third and youngest of the “Cursed women of Eve". She has always appeared the the most reserved and reticent of the sisters, watching her new existence go by from the safety of her bedroom room window. Although her new life is confusing, Flame's presence, albeit from afar has always been a comfort to her and when she hears that her saviour may need saving, she doesn’t hesitate to be there for him. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438897600ra/15768503.gif" width="400" alt=" photo D0617863-307F-4632-A07A-1725E68B042B_zpsdal1qu7p.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is one of my annoying non-reviews. Reason being, I truly feel it's a story that needs to be experienced. It's intense. Did I mention it was intense? I was however grateful for the uplifting ending for Flame and Maddie. As for the sneak peak into Cain/Rider's book, the story there is far from other over.<br><br><b>“I used to wonder how two people—one broken girl, and one broken boy—could ever move on from their dark and tortured pasts. But now I know. Together, that’s how. They fight their way through… together.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438892766i/15767837._SX540_.jpg" width="400"   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1358287439" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1358287439?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1358287439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9063979553256174552"><br/>I think I say this in every review for Tillie’s book, but she continues to blow my mind. How she is able to deliver such unique, diverse stories through so many different genres amazes me. I remember the first time I met her at a signing I was shocked to see <i>Sweet Home</i> sitting next to <i>It Ain’t Me Babe.</i> I am super embarrassing so I actually said this thought out loud…to her. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>She was special to me. She was everything. She was all I thought about, day and night. I had to be underneath her w</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText9063979553256174552" style="display:none"><br>I think I say this in every review for Tillie’s book, but she continues to blow my mind. How she is able to deliver such unique, diverse stories through so many different genres amazes me. I remember the first time I met her at a signing I was shocked to see <i>Sweet Home</i> sitting next to <i>It Ain’t Me Babe.</i> I am super embarrassing so I actually said this thought out loud…to her. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>She was special to me. She was everything. She was all I thought about, day and night. I had to be underneath her window just to be near her. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>From the first moment I met Flame I was taken by him. There was just something about this damaged man and I needed to know what made him the way he was. Now, after reading Flame’s story the only thing I can say is my heart truly broke for him. Flame was raised similar to Maddie, in that they were both brain washed by others interruptions of the Bible. Their family’s faiths destroyed them as people. <br><br>Now it has been years and Flame cannot stand to be touched by another person for fear he will destroy them. Maddie cannot stand to be touched by men for fear of what they will do to her, but together they can heal each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439348731i/15825140._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wish I was able to write a review that would do this story justice, because to say two broken people came together and healed each other is such a huge understatement. Flame and Maddie’s connection is just more. There is no other way to truly express it than to say they are more. They are each other’s other half. They are the person who gets them like no one else can. Maddie can speak to Flame on another level and his fierce need to protect her and be there for her, motivates him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439348731i/15825141._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It’s no secret I am a huge Tillie Cole fan, but this story blew my mind. It was everything I was hoping for and so much more. <i>Souls Unfractured</i> is a beautiful, heartbreaking, soul crushing story that will break you, but will also lift your heart in such a way you believe in Maddie and Flame’s love. Their love is never ending, it is unconditional, it is perfect. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439348731i/15825142._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>
  <a href="http://readingissexybookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574955.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
<br>
  <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Reading-is-Sexy-Book-Blog/717861984979600" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574956.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1204618432" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1204618432?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=fighters-and-bad-asses">fighters-and-bad-asses</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cat-heart-these-books">cat-heart-these-books</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1204618432" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4148566268938187391"><b>5 Amazing Stars.</b>	<br/><br/>This book (finally) bring us the story of Flame and Maddie. Flame is obsessed with Maddie since he first laid eyes on her, but with his past still ruling him it’s hard to approach people, especially people like Maddie he thinks his undeserving of. But Maddie, also a girl broken by her abusive and controlling past, is decided to show him that they can’t be good together and that sometimes fighting ghosts together is better than fighting them alone. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440714229i/16013540.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Saying that I’ve been anxious </span>
  <span id="freeText4148566268938187391" style="display:none"><b>5 Amazing Stars.</b>	<br><br>This book (finally) bring us the story of Flame and Maddie. Flame is obsessed with Maddie since he first laid eyes on her, but with his past still ruling him it’s hard to approach people, especially people like Maddie he thinks his undeserving of. But Maddie, also a girl broken by her abusive and controlling past, is decided to show him that they can’t be good together and that sometimes fighting ghosts together is better than fighting them alone. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440714229i/16013540.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Saying that I’ve been anxious for this book since I’ve met Flame and Maddie is an understatement. I could barely wait for their book. And I’ve got to say it didn’t disappoint at all! Amazingly written, emotional, sometimes heart wrenching to read but completely worth every minute of reading. If you’re a fan of the series you can’t miss this book… and if you haven’t read these books yet, you should really start now. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429744792i/14626262.jpg" width="350" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 Stars.<br> <b>Characters Development: </b> We already knew that Flame was a broken man and I was anxious to know what happen in his past that made him broken like that, and I’ve got to say that was amazing to finally see the “real” Flame and it was impossible not to love the broken and obsessed Flame. Maddie was also broken, but still it was amazing how caring she was with Flame. These are all incredibly strong girls. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Mental and physical abuse. Violence.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText15817617037219209338" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>4 Stars</b> ★★★★ <br><br><b>Now LIVE!<br>Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.com/B013OJYRJI">http://amzn.com/B013OJYRJI</a><br>Amazon UK - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1J5PRuQ">http://amzn.to/1J5PRuQ</a></b><br><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439025277i/15783551._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I honestly don't know where to start, this book was one hell of an intense read and I am in awe of how Tillie Cole has written a story so emotionally deep and heartbreaking, and at the same time made us fall in love with these broken characters who end up becoming such a strong and unbreakable couple.<br><br>Flame is different from most people, throughout the series we have seen how he self harms and how he finds it hard to relate to others. He is intimidating and unpredictable but when he meets young Maddie, he becomes something else, protective.<br><br>Maddie is the youngest of the sisters, and also the most broken. From the age of six she was abused by the elders within the order and subjected to the most awful crimes. However, she is strong and it is her who is the one to finally calm the flames that live inside of Flame.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439295564i/15817986._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Flame's story is absolutely devastating and quite hard to read at times, but he turned out to be one of the sweetest hero's that I have ever read. His feelings for Maddie are so wonderfully pure that you can't help but swoon and smile when he fights his awkwardness and speaks of his feelings towards her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I need her."<br>I tapped my head.<br>"In here, I need her."<br>Then I bounced my fist over my heart.<br>"And here, I feel her in here too."</b>
</blockquote> <br>Amongst the dark themes of this book, there is a beautiful love story and the love is not limited to Flame and Maddie, but also within the brotherhood. AK and Viking really shone through for me in this book, they love him just as strongly.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"He's Flame. He's my fucking brother, condition or not."</b>
</blockquote> <br>Also, we had a few chapters from Rider's/Prophet Cain's POV and let me tell you that his book is going to be a hell of a ride, The redemption has begun!<br><br>So, if you are a fully fledged fan of this series, there is no doubt you will love this one. It was pretty close to perfect and although the subject matter was truly gruesome, it was necessary to go there in order for us to really feel the pain that Flame and Maddie went though to become the adults they were today.<br><br>Bravo Tillie, this series is turning out to be an Epic one.<br><br><b>Told in dual POV, this is the third book in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/128581-hades-hangmen" rel="nofollow noopener">Hades Hangmen series</a>.</b> <br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an honest review</i> <br> <br><a href="http://ilovebooklove-ab.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1175620163" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1175620163" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1175620163?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=mc">mc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1175620163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14386653893151033252"><b>5 Burn for Me Stars</b><br/><br/>I love Tillie Cole and I love the Hades Hangmen series. Souls Unfractured is a standalone because each book focuses on a new character, but you should read the series from the beginning to get the full effect. Maddie and Flame’s presence is huge in the previous books. I felt like the first two books were foreplay to their relationship and YAY we finally get to their story.<br/><br/>Maddie was tortured and rape repeatedly by the men in the Order. Because of this, she can’t handle men’s p</span>
  <span id="freeText14386653893151033252" style="display:none"><b>5 Burn for Me Stars</b><br><br>I love Tillie Cole and I love the Hades Hangmen series. Souls Unfractured is a standalone because each book focuses on a new character, but you should read the series from the beginning to get the full effect. Maddie and Flame’s presence is huge in the previous books. I felt like the first two books were foreplay to their relationship and YAY we finally get to their story.<br><br>Maddie was tortured and rape repeatedly by the men in the Order. Because of this, she can’t handle men’s presence (as she shouldn’t). Flame has to cut himself to function. He feels burns throughout his body and the only way to release this is by cutting.<br><br>As you can see, this is not an easy book to read. Both Maddie and Flame are tortured souls and I greedily and happily wanted to read their story. Tillie had me at page one and I never wanted to stop reading. She gave me everything I wanted and more. I felt pure sadness, hurt, anger and love.<br><br>You will feel a lot of emotions when you read this book. You will weep for Flame and his crazy heart. You will be inspired by Maddie and root for her to feel safe and happy. Each time Flame and Maddie interact, I was on pins and needles. I wondered how Flame would react towards her and how Maddie would react towards Flame. I never wanted a couple to work out as I did with them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The flames never calmed. They forever … burned. But with her… I wanted to grip her tighter”<br><br>“I like to watch you. I like you being near me. It’s better than standing under your window. I like being able to see you up close.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The thing that really MADE this story is the back story and EVERYTHING that lead up to THEM. I loved reading about Flame (even though it was very difficult), I needed to know what made him the way he is. The things Flames does to cope is so troubled. I loved how “different” Flame was too. He doesn’t react nor speak like everyone else. It made me love him just a touch more. Tillie never fails to amaze me. I loved Maddie’s reaction towards Flame. I love her soft to his hard, her sweetness to his spice, her light to his dark. Maddie and Flame balanced each other perfectly.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You are a good man,<br> Flame. You were simply dealt a bad hand.” <br><br>“I knew he would not lie. He could not lie. That made me feel safe. And to me, feeling safe was the most important thing in my life.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>You get some of the old characters too and it’s nice to tie everyone together. You also get bits of Cain’s POV and you can make your assumptions about that (it’s an eye opener).<br><br>I waited months for this story, I stalked Tillie’s Facebook, blog and group anticipating for this book. I never placed so much hype as I did on this one and after I read it, all I felt was boom … explosions. She’s gifted, talented and I can’t wait what she has in stored for us next.<br><br><br><i>An ARC was provided</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22020052.It_Ain_t_Me__Babe__Hades_Hangmen___1_" title="It Ain't Me, Babe (Hades Hangmen, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1398707039s/22020052.jpg" alt="It Ain't Me, Babe (Hades Hangmen, #1) by Tillie Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1415799095s/22107044.jpg" alt="Heart Recaptured (Hades Hangmen, #2) by Tillie Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> Heart Recaptured <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/957441256" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00QZLSQ9U/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00QZLSQ9U&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=4FPZYG6DF3SGBMID" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418747192i/12887523.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22107214.Souls_Unfractured__Hades_Hangmen___3_" title="Souls Unfractured (Hades Hangmen, #3) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1992342091" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1992342091" />
    <a title="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34454544-alicia"><img alt="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480986441p2/34454544.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1992342091?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ " href="/user/show/34454544-alicia">⊱✿⊰ Alicia ⊱✿⊰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=2017-favs">2017-favs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=2017-dark-reads">2017-dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=biker">biker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=2017-twisted-reads">2017-twisted-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=2017-5-star">2017-5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=3rd-in-series">3rd-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34454544-alicia?shelf=religion">religion</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1992342091" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11016700370604375991"><b>5 <i>Gut-Wrenching</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/guyonfire_zpsoqewlwun.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494679430ra/22739009.gif' alt=' photo guyonfire_zpsoqewlwun.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"For fractured souls are like magnets. Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss..."</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>What a depressingly raw and beautiful love story. Maddie and Flame are messed up!! I mean Flame cuts himself non-stop with huge knives and will not let anyone touch him as he thinks the flames within his veins will hurt them. Flames story is just gut wrenching and being a mother of a special needs child made it a little close to home especially when the 'R' word was used, I can't deal</span>
  <span id="freeText11016700370604375991" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>Gut-Wrenching</i> Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/guyonfire_zpsoqewlwun.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494679430ra/22739009.gif" alt=" photo guyonfire_zpsoqewlwun.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"For fractured souls are like magnets. Drawn to collide into an impossible bliss..."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>What a depressingly raw and beautiful love story. Maddie and Flame are messed up!! I mean Flame cuts himself non-stop with huge knives and will not let anyone touch him as he thinks the flames within his veins will hurt them. Flames story is just gut wrenching and being a mother of a special needs child made it a little close to home especially when the 'R' word was used, I can't deal with that word.<br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/crying_zpsfbuhup8z.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494679430ra/22739010.gif" alt=" photo crying_zpsfbuhup8z.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maddie being one of the 'cursed' has lived through her own hell but I actually think she is the most level headed one out of the three 'cursed' sisters. Apart from not letting anyone touch her and her fear of men, she seems to have a stronger grip on reality about the fact they had been brainwashed growing up.<br><br>I have to say one thing though, the first sex scene between these two was just a little weird and 100% <b>AWKWARD!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/awkward-gif_zpszwrjekz0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494679430ra/22739011.gif" alt=" photo awkward-gif_zpszwrjekz0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I had to put it down for a bit during the scene to clear my head ;)<br><br>As with the second book I enjoyed the few chapters we got from New Zion. It is told from Cain's POV he is the new profit of the 'order' and he is one sad guy, he was raised isolated far from the commune and forced to learn everything about the 'orders' fucked up religion. Although he was not taught everything and he is slowly starting to believe there may be something shady going on. Well DUH!! ya think??<br><br>So this was definitely more of a love story between two very lost souls rather than an MC read in my opinion. Not that it matters as it was amazing. I still got all the characters from the MC and enough club 'stuff' to keep me interested in what will happen next in the series.<br><br>I highly recommend this series :)<br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/neverletmego_zpswpecivao.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494679430ra/22739012.gif" alt=" photo neverletmego_zpswpecivao.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/5startemplate_zps27mqg0f6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491829369i/22451184._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5startemplate_zps27mqg0f6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11016700370604375991" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_18739485'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18739485-king"><img alt="King (King, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1434996511l/18739485._SX98_.jpg" />

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DvyKVVYO0Md4QDohWmM4bj+bl4gwV53UikvnL1M1RrzsdO7n2Znvnc1PaUCJUrNiXdrogy60tyeqAAMBk4Fe2w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wgPUqikah9Lsq4nY7SoKsefFsmueH2wbEJzAhNdUZV8gi7AYpo24iFmk2rk+G4G9hYTNYID8Rugw1ySqF+B9OA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">About Tillie Cole</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1517004382p3/7074846.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">Tillie Cole
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
13,959
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9682827229456175592">Amazon & USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses.</span>
  <span id="freeText9682827229456175592" style="display:none">Amazon &amp; USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses. <br />Being a scary blend of Scottish and English, Tillie embraces both cultures; her English heritage through her love of HP sauce and freshly made Yorkshire Puddings, and her Scottish which is mostly demonstrated by her frighteningly foul-mouthed episodes of pure rage and her much loved dirty jokes.<br /><br />Having been born and raised as a Teesside Smoggie, Tillie, at age nineteen, moved forty miles north to the 'Toon', Newcastle-Upon-Tyne, where she attended Newcastle University and graduated with a Bachelor of Arts honours degree in Religious Studies. She returned two years later to complete a Post-Graduate Certificate in Teaching High School Social Studies. Tillie, regards Newcastle to be a home from home and enjoyed the Newcastle Geordie way of life for seven 'proper mint' and 'lush' years.<br /><br />One summers day, after finishing reading her thousandth book on her much loved and treasured Kindle, Tillie turned to her husband and declared, "D'you know, I have a great idea for a story. I could write a book." Several months later, after repeating the same tired line at the close of another completed story, she was scolded by her husband to shut up talking about writing a novel and "just bloody do it!" For the first time in eleven years, Tillie actually took his advice (he is still trying to get over the shock) and immediately set off on a crazy journey, delving deep into her fertile imagination. <br /><br />Tillie, ever since, has written from the heart. She combines her passion for anything camp and glittery with her love of humour and dark brooding men (most often muscled and tattooed – they’re her weakness!). She also has a serious side (believe it or not!) and loves to immerse herself in the complex study of World Religions, History and Cultural Studies and creates fantasy stories that enable her to thread serious issues and topics into her writing -- yep, there's more to this girl than profanity and sparkles!<br /><br />After six years of teaching high school Social Studies and following her Professional Rugby Player husband around Europe, they have finally given up their nomadic way of life and settled in Calgary, Alberta where Tillie spends most of her days (and many a late night) lost in a writing euphoria or pursuing a dazzling career as a barrel-racing, tasselled-chap wearing, Stetson-sporting cowgirl... Ye-haw!<br /></span>
